
-----title
洛阳（西京） (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2d47afbef2fe4f34be64351165a927da_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2d47afbef2fe4f34be64351165a927da");'><span id='2d47afbef2fe4f34be64351165a927da_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1022')">1004-1022年</a>，1-19岁</div><div id='2d47afbef2fe4f34be64351165a927da' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年1月1日</a>　本年出生。出生地不详，姑系籍贯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1006')">1005-1006年</a>　居河南。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年</a>　居河南。与邻家幼儿玩，遇打雷不惊，被称为有异才。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1009')">1008-1009年</a>　居河南。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1010&endYear=1015')">1010-1015年</a>　居河南。在书院习读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年</a>　居河南。在书院习读。时第三妹出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1019')">1017-1019年</a>　居河南。在书院习读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1021')">1020-1021年</a>　居河南。读书于天宫寺三学院。有大志。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1022&endYear=1022')">1022年1月</a>　居洛阳。父富言加升太常博士。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='faa08ebbb00a426e906a19886e058772_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("faa08ebbb00a426e906a19886e058772");'><span id='faa08ebbb00a426e906a19886e058772_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1033')">1031-1033年</a>，28-30岁</div><div id='faa08ebbb00a426e906a19886e058772' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年11月</a>　本月捧父富言骨灰回洛阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　在洛阳丁忧。时梅尧臣由河南县主簿改任河阳县主簿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年11月6日</a>　十一月初六，葬于洛阳县北.<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年11月</a>　居家丁忧。十一月应人之请作《燕堂记》。<div id='poem_1159548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>燕堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（明道二年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159548")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159548'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159548'>佐著作乐君宰福昌，筑室署下，走使问名于余，且揭地图以来谒辞为志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159548_comment'></div>按图，福昌古宜阳地，战国韩所都，西压秦境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159548_comment'></div>二国争胜相攻取，此为兵冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159548_comment'></div>西南有山，极高，似熊耳，汉樊贼委甲齐之，是则古鲑壤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159548_comment'></div>二京往来，南路近出县侧，人甚嚣坌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159548_comment'></div>世以迥，故径取崤渑为东西道，由是此路遂僻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159548_comment'></div>今人举洛都寰内邑，历历独福昌居胜绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159548_comment'></div>二山夹起，迤逦西去，轪耸如峙，河流在中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159548_comment'></div>乡人浚其流以莳稻，横斜潴亩，枝骛脉散，为畦为陇，为沟浍，为堤塍，方方如棋者愈数万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159548_comment'></div>厥田膏沃，多丘陵原冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159548_comment'></div>厥植多竹，多松柏，于近水多蒲蕖蕙芷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159548_comment'></div>厥兽多熊，多麝麇麋，厥鸟多鹥鹊鹏鹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159548_comment'></div>山水重砯，气色秀润，不假御桴舟、驰惊澜而坐见江山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159548_comment'></div>又风俗富腴，人情舒闲，耕者渔者，或旁山趾，或临水缦，与野物杂居，不识鲑争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159548_comment'></div>乐君长于治剧，至是法令罕任，收志静虑而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159548_comment'></div>一日得厅背露地，诛丛薄，发石磔，成为洁壤，乃作是室，以纳休燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159548_comment'></div>林木逶邃，左右回合，前有池纵广裁百尺，水色溶漾，风去如炮，飞梁跨越，渴虹下饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159548_comment'></div>池中有亭曰「凝碧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159548_comment'></div>后倚山，曲折而上，凡数十步，胁间有亭曰「凌云」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159548_comment'></div>周旋环视，群峰插天，相连无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159548_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159548_comment'></div>不出户庭而所得之景如游千万里外，思水则临前池，思山则登后亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159548_comment'></div>登临既倦，于是止而憩，偃而寐，起而吟盳以笑，图书琴瑟，玩好古器，莫不具在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159548_comment'></div>熙熙融融，不知景物之怡乎性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159548_comment'></div>娱燕如此，命名曰「燕堂」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159548_comment'></div>堂东西五楹，南北五椽，任材之质，不以藻画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159548_comment'></div>自始兴工至毕，凡二十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159548_comment'></div>明道二年冬日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1159548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159548'><span class='label'>按：</span>《古今图书集成》职方典卷四四一。又见同书考工典卷五八。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1159548_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a0f9f41f96a944d6b238956fb62df265_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a0f9f41f96a944d6b238956fb62df265");'><span id='a0f9f41f96a944d6b238956fb62df265_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>，31岁</div><div id='a0f9f41f96a944d6b238956fb62df265' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年夏末</a>　夏末回洛阳。秋，欧阳修来书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　本年上疏奏论阅将、募兵、救荒、弥寇等事。不纳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　本年三妹嫁田况，时年十九。田况为楚州团练判官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b3b5fdc55f7144f1b3473c79e4a26d8d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b3b5fdc55f7144f1b3473c79e4a26d8d");'><span id='b3b5fdc55f7144f1b3473c79e4a26d8d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1063')">1061-1063年</a>，58-60岁</div><div id='b3b5fdc55f7144f1b3473c79e4a26d8d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年3月16日</a>　因母丧去位归洛阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年3月17日</a>　朝廷因富弼母丧罢春宴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年6月23日</a>　诏起复，不拜，上辞表，从之。作品：《辞起复表》<div id='poem_1159468' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159468' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159468?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞起复表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年6月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159468")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159468_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159468'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159468'>丧次衔哀，甫终卒哭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159468_comment'></div>使华传命，继至弊庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159468_comment'></div>心积惊忧，情深屠裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159468_comment'></div>虽屡倾于丹恳，尚未锡于俞音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159468_comment'></div>天远莫量，物微难动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159468_comment'></div>不避亵烦之咎，更陈陨绝之词，必冀神聪，俯从哀请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159468_comment'></div>伏念臣早罹家难，偏奉母慈，猥以蠢愚，最钟爱育，享禄未几，遽缠风树之悲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159468_comment'></div>报德永违，徒怀霜露之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159468_comment'></div>寖苫枕块而适抱至痛，食稻衣锦则若为自安，实非人情，尤紊邦制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159468_comment'></div>况今中外无事，左右得贤，共辅圣明之期，安有隳旷之务？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159468_comment'></div>曲蒙下诏，更起孤臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159468_comment'></div>在陛下驭国之方，盖欲不遗于旧物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159468_comment'></div>于朝廷敦化之道，必恐有误于苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159468_comment'></div>何须稽故事以遂前世之非，正可存礼经以图今日之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159468_comment'></div>行之即是，义不为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159468_comment'></div>岂惟于陛下有复古之风，抑亦俾愚臣得事亲之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159468_comment'></div>一为匪戾，两得其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159468_comment'></div>兼臣悲伤之馀，衰病交至，精力已耗，神观未还，假使充员，岂堪应务？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159468_comment'></div>苟令终毕于祥禫，庶几稍复于干魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159468_comment'></div>得此从容，可备驱策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159468_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下日月临照，天地包容，尽母氏平生之恩，怜人子罔极之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159468_comment'></div>曲矜末志，得满钜忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159468_comment'></div>生意凋零，或尚未捐于沟壑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159468_comment'></div>清光咫尺，终期伏望于云天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159468_comment'></div>悲感增深，恳愿兼剧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1159468_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　上两奏。作品：《论张述不合升奖奏》《言求嗣不可过急奏》<div id='poem_1159502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论张述不合升奖奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐六年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159502")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159502'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159502'>窃闻新授提点银铜场、职方员外郎张述累有封章，乞立储贰，其词太过，颇涉匪彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159502_comment'></div>事合婉微，述乃伤于逼迫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159502_comment'></div>语当秘密，述乃极于张皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159502_comment'></div>传闻四方，无不惊骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159502_comment'></div>伏缘张述前知泗州，绝无政举，臣在中书日，亦曾见其阙失事状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159502_comment'></div>本官必是恐朝廷不用，遂强作此事，虽云纳忠而献直，实掩过以取名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159502_comment'></div>果若忧国爱君，岂肯如此喧布！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159502_comment'></div>况提点银铜场，将来例入职司，如述小人，不合升奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159502_comment'></div>臣切恐好进之辈，更相仿效，妄陈祸福，频挠圣聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159502_comment'></div>陛下或致忧隐，切于求嗣，即于天听，却成不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159502_comment'></div>臣今虽不在陛下左右，实则日久忧虑，寝食不安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159502_comment'></div>且念自古帝王未有不任情喜怒，杀害臣民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159502_comment'></div>恭惟陛下临御已四十年，未尝枉怒一人，况于刑诛，固无分毫枉滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159502_comment'></div>惟是仁慈宽恕，甚于父母之爱赤子，天下蒙被陛下大恩大惠，深入骨髓，上苍观览，岂无报应！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159502_comment'></div>明知圣嗣非晚降育，臣今所愿者，惟愿陛下勤于政事之外，凡百节谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159502_comment'></div>目前爱玩，多方制伏其心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159502_comment'></div>至于宴饮间动风发气之物，亦宜拣择，不令进御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159502_comment'></div>澄神静思，助以平和之药，必享万寿无疆之庆，永为宗社之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159502_comment'></div>皇嗣之晚，未足为虑，此乃必然之理也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1159502_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1159503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159503?labeling=true' target='_blank'>言求嗣不可过急奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐六年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159503")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159503'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159503'>窃恐陛下左右亲近者，知陛下求嗣心切，一向希宠望幸，各有诞育之意，人人争进，则陛下虽欲制伏其心，不可得也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159503_comment'></div>虽欲保惜圣躬，亦不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159503_comment'></div>如此，则臣实为陛下忧之，为宗庙社稷忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159503_comment'></div>臣尝为上相，义同股肱，当与国家共其祸福，不得不忧及此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159503_comment'></div>陛下若不以臣为狂妄，即乞以臣此意，一一宣谕亲近之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159503_comment'></div>臣必料亲近者皆有保惜圣躬之心，各便省悟，而能长守富贵，即于陛下，自然无忧，实天下之幸也，宗庙社稷之幸也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159503_comment'></div>圣嗣既系天命，自有天时，不可以人力强致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159503_comment'></div>臣受陛下深恩，出于恳切，不觉语及于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159503_comment'></div>臣不敢避死，陛下若肯听纳，然后赐臣以死，实亦甘心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1159503_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年闰8月25日</a>　诏给月俸之半，不受。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　本年有与蔡襄贴。作品：《修建坟院贴》<div id='poem_1159545' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159545' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159545?labeling=true' target='_blank'>修建坟院帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159545")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159545_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159545'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159545'>弼修建坟院，得额已久，先人神刻，理当崇立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159545_comment'></div>今天下文章，惟君谟与永叔主之，又生平最相知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159545_comment'></div>永叔方执政，不欲干请，独有意于君谟久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159545_comment'></div>但为编次文字未就，故且迁延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159545_comment'></div>昨因示谕，辄敢预闻下执，即非发于偶然，惟故人□察，少安下情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159545_comment'></div>皇恐皇恐！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159545_comment'></div>院榜候得，请别上闻，复《圆觉偈》，亦如教刊模也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159545_comment'></div>哀感何胜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159545_comment'></div>哀感何胜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159545_comment'></div>弼又上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159545_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1159545'>温柑绝新好，尽荐于几筵，悲感悲感！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159545_comment'></div>弼又启。</div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年2月28日</a>　韩琦判相州，有贺书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年夏</a>　陈襄来启。<br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年3月</a>　王安石复相。本月上奏答复北边事宜。作品：《答诏问北边事宜奏》<div id='poem_1159524' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159524' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159524?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答诏问北边事宜奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁八年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159524")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159524_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159524'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159524'>臣素乏才业，忝尘二府，昔在壮时，精力尚不及人，今老且病，气志衰耗，何足备大政之问？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159524_comment'></div>然臣实非己见，今但举众人所得闻者录以上奏，惟圣明裁择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159524_comment'></div>臣五六年来，切闻绥州、娄、熙河、辰、锦、戎、泸、交趾，咸议用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159524_comment'></div>唯交趾中寝，其馀诸路，皆有攻讨，或尅获，或丧失，即传播天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159524_comment'></div>而绥州、娄、熙河，始初兴举，便传闻云朝廷必复灵、夏，平贺兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159524_comment'></div>既又大传有人上平燕之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159524_comment'></div>此说尤盛，北狄必已探知相备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159524_comment'></div>复传闻朝廷修整器甲，简练兵伍，增筑城垒，积聚刍粮，加之招致高丽为牵制之援，近又分置河北三十六将，按阅愈急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159524_comment'></div>喧布渐久，事机参合，此敌人所以先期启衅，以发代北侵境之端而不肯已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159524_comment'></div>其平贺兰、平燕之策，虚实固不可知，然传者既多且久，万口一词，谁敢辨白？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159524_comment'></div>设有辨者，远夷何以取信？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159524_comment'></div>今衅端已成，代北各屯兵马境上，争议逾年未决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159524_comment'></div>横使再至，事归朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159524_comment'></div>此边城之职，而朝廷自当之，则恐理难欸缓，便要可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159524_comment'></div>违之则兵立起而患速，顺之则河东斥堠窄狭，为患虽迟而久远不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159524_comment'></div>臣谓不若一委边臣，令其坚持久来图籍疆界为据，使其尽力交相诘难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159524_comment'></div>然北狄非不自知理曲，盖故欲生事，遂兴干戈，以气吞我，以势陵我，是欲夺我累年所作之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159524_comment'></div>彼非敢无故骤兴此端，实有以致其来也，惟陛下深省熟虑，不可独谓敌人结衅背盟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159524_comment'></div>彼若万一入寇，事不得已，我持严兵以待之，来则御战，去则备守，此自古中国防边之要也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159524_comment'></div>若朝廷乘忿，便欲深入讨击，臣实虑万一蹉跌，其害非细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159524_comment'></div>更或与西夏为犄角之势，则朝廷宵旰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159524_comment'></div>事既至此，边奏警急，兵粮皆缺，窘于应用，须防四方凶徒，必有观望者，谓国家方事外虞，其力不能制我，遂相啸聚，蜂猬而起，事将奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159524_comment'></div>臣愿陛下以宗社为忧，生民为念，纳污含垢，且求安静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159524_comment'></div>更俟岁时丰稔，穷困稍苏，流亡渐归，民粗安业，税赋不失，仓廪不虚，恩信宣布，人心固结，然后别图万全之举，贵免一跌之失，此天下之愿也，亦臣之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159524_comment'></div>向又喧传陛下决为亲征之谋，中外益更忧惧，心殒胆落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159524_comment'></div>陛下虽英睿天纵，必有成算，然太平天子与创业之君，事体绝异，尤不可概然轻举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159524_comment'></div>又恐朝廷且作声势，固无实心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159524_comment'></div>事若如此，乃是我以虚声而邀彼实来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159524_comment'></div>张虚声者必有疏略之虞，作实来者必有周密之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159524_comment'></div>以疏略之虞而当周密之计，其成败岂不灼然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159524_comment'></div>假令入讨得志而还，此契丹一种，事力自大，况夏国、置勒斯赉、高丽、黑水、女真、达靼等诸蕃为之党援，其势必难殄灭，使无噍类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159524_comment'></div>即由此结成边患，卒无已时，大非长辔远驭之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159524_comment'></div>臣切谓因横使之来，且可选人以其疑我者数事开怀喻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159524_comment'></div>云朝廷凡所为武备，乃中国常事，非愿外兴征伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159524_comment'></div>向者用武之地，皆小蕃有过者，朝廷须合问罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159524_comment'></div>若吾二大邦通好，已是七十馀年，无故安肯辄欲破坏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159524_comment'></div>恐是奸人造作，妄兴间谍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159524_comment'></div>或是彼闻我整肃边事，即疑我有所兴作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159524_comment'></div>我既知之，岂免大为准拟？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159524_comment'></div>盖因此互相疑惑，养成衅隙，遂有今日争理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159524_comment'></div>朝廷更有可说诸事，但尽说之，须令释然无惑，乃一助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159524_comment'></div>横使始不纳，即遣报聘者，于戎主前具道此意，庶几一听，必有所益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159524_comment'></div>缘彼大藉朝廷岁与，方成国计，既有顾藉之心，岂无安静之欲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159524_comment'></div>只以疑情未释，遂成倔强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159524_comment'></div>若与开解明白，必肯回心向化，凡百芥蒂，尽可脱略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159524_comment'></div>茍互相疑忌，两情不通，祸患日深，必成后悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159524_comment'></div>臣历观春秋洎战国时，诸侯递相征伐，两兵已合，飞矢在上，行人在下，辨说解释，遂各交缔而退却，复盟好者，比比皆是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159524_comment'></div>况今衅端渐启，兵尚未合，且可多方以理解释，或能有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159524_comment'></div>与其用征战而决胜负，万万不侔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159524_comment'></div>彼此致疑及御戎二事，臣并得之群论，非出胸臆，是皆目前众所共知、所共见，必然之理，非事外别生奇异之策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159524_comment'></div>臣更望陛下兼求博访，不宜专听一偏之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159524_comment'></div>恐有迎合圣意及畏避用事之人，不敢尽以实事上奏，有误国家大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159524_comment'></div>臣今所以及此者，切闻去春以久旱，陛下特降手诏，许人极陈朝政得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159524_comment'></div>中外欢抃，咸谓圣情已大开悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159524_comment'></div>寻闻上章论列者甚多，随而或遭贬降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159524_comment'></div>陛下殊不以手诏召人极谏为意而优容之，反令得罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159524_comment'></div>士大夫自此皆务钳结，忠荩之语，不敢复出于口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159524_comment'></div>臣谓下情不能上达者，乃朝政莫大之患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159524_comment'></div>愿陛下深思极虑之，早令天下受赐，及朝廷无事，不胜大幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159524_comment'></div>此奏出于匆遽，又且欲事理明白，不敢加饰及援据古事，但直书利害而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159524_comment'></div>昔楚相子反谓区区之宋，尚有不欺人之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159524_comment'></div>况中原大国，已与北寇结隙，今若更不推诚以待之，则恐不能解疑释惑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159524_comment'></div>伏乞圣造，特加裁恕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1159524_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年10月29日</a>　十月初七，有彗星出。第二日诏臣僚建言。二十九日富弼有奏。作品：《答诏论彗星奏》<div id='poem_1159525' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159525' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159525?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答诏论彗星奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁八年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年10月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159525")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159525_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159525'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159525'>臣伏念向缘衰疾，加之年已及格，不能奔走职事，遂求致政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159525_comment'></div>伏蒙圣慈，俯从愚恳，退处衡茅之下，杜门自守，屏绝私务，朝夕待尽而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159525_comment'></div>近日忽闻特宣大赦，出于非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159525_comment'></div>又闻别降手诏，许中外臣寮直言朝政阙失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159525_comment'></div>洛城士庶，欢呼鼓舞，喧于道路，声彻幽远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159525_comment'></div>推是而往，则天下之人无不感动矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159525_comment'></div>臣伏览赦诏二文，始以彗星东出，昭示谴告，陛下仰观天变，恐惧疚怀，浚发德音，恩霈寰海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159525_comment'></div>臣固知一出圣断，必无左右之助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159525_comment'></div>臣再详陛下手诏，乃陛下亲笔，非学士所作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159525_comment'></div>以至比年灾异，如山摧、地震、旱蝗之类，前后包括，一一归咎于己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159525_comment'></div>辞旨哀痛，深切明白，忠义之士，读之莫不感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159525_comment'></div>而又避正殿、减常膳、设斋醮、屏侍御，前代帝王禳灾弭患、责躬罪己之法，陛下尽行之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159525_comment'></div>所以上天降鉴，知陛下发于至诚，故星变不旋踵而灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159525_comment'></div>臣温衣饱食，坐享安佚，灾祸之至，殊无干及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159525_comment'></div>一见圣诏骤发，即日感动天地，谴异消伏，速如影响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159525_comment'></div>臣尚能踊跃欣蹈，不知纪极，彼天下之人身被灾害，家罹荼毒，流落破散，不能相保者，其为欢喜感戴，当何如也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159525_comment'></div>人心既喜，和气充塞，则天意不得不早回，天灾不得不遄息，此理固然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159525_comment'></div>臣窃知去年久旱，陛下曾降手诏，许臣寮上封论事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159525_comment'></div>人方喜悦，日俟朝廷施设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159525_comment'></div>而不知何人者，上累圣德，遽成反汗，于是天下大失所望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159525_comment'></div>臣近于三月中，仰答圣问，略曾引及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159525_comment'></div>今天变益大，诏命益切，陛下万必不复蹈前车之误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159525_comment'></div>况诏云「朝政阙失，朕将虚心以改」，此足见圣意畏天爱民，其已至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159525_comment'></div>然臣窃闻外议，皆云天下弊病甚众，官家多应不知，人人咸愿条列，达于天听，冀幸有所刬革尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159525_comment'></div>已大发圣诏，许其开陈，忠愤者必能不避诛戮，仰竭肝胆，悉以上闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159525_comment'></div>臣愿陛下尽取群奏，不遗疏贱，万几之暇，一一亲阅，择其众说，所合者断在不惑，力赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159525_comment'></div>践虚心以改之辞，应天文尤大之变，使泽及普率，急若置邮，则人心悦，天道顺，天人相应，立致和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159525_comment'></div>国家享无疆之休者，正在此时也，岂复有灾眚出见，而上骇圣虑哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159525_comment'></div>万一奸诈互入，宸听少惑，俾夫忠告为妄说，恩诏为空文，利泽不出于上，人心复愁于下，则天将曰是以虚辞答我，迄无实效，必回今日之喜，翻为异日之怒，灾变之作，当又甚于前日之慧者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159525_comment'></div>但以近事證之，此乃必然之理，非臣辄敢狂率也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159525_comment'></div>惟望陛下深赐裁察，为宗庙社稷生灵之计，不胜天下大幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159525_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1159525'>〔手劄子〕臣未致仕前，虽有旧疾，筋力粗可驱策，尚不能从官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159525_comment'></div>今致仕已数年，衰老益甚，退伏草野，未尝与人相接，荣辱祸福，都不干预，而辄敢以狂瞽之说，妄陈天听者，实见陛下仰观星变，恐惧修省，若不自容也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159525_comment'></div>又闻天下生民，穷困已甚，无所伸诉，恐成啸聚，为腹心之患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159525_comment'></div>亦虑手诏或致中废，天谴未息，则后来别生灾害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159525_comment'></div>臣所以不顾身之老病而彊作此奏，庶几有所补助，而报陛下大恩之万一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159525_comment'></div>缘臣閒居终日，与野老相见，民间弊病，盈塞耳目，皆是实事，然所说者，尚未尽一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159525_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈，略赐省鉴，而少留圣意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159525_comment'></div>臣又辄敢烦陛下亲阅群奏者，若委臣寮置局，必恐不能上体圣意忧劳之切，群奏中利害有所不尽，亦恐所委臣寮更存顾望，尚或隐蔽，或陈巧说，妄有沮难，则误圣君畏天爱民、不吝改悔之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159525_comment'></div>臣固无他肠，所忧者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159525_comment'></div>惟望陛下，特赐矜察，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1159525_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年4月</a>　有上疏，论时政。作品：《论时政疏》<div id='poem_1159526' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159526' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159526?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论时政疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁九年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159526")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159526_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159526'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159526'>臣近者因拜谢章，辄敢略具南事附奏，伏计愚恳，寻达天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159526_comment'></div>蛮寇大扰，即已窜归，然王师遂行，必谋吊伐，水陆并进，威德兼施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159526_comment'></div>若夫讨御之方，得失之际，则非臣庸之所预知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159526_comment'></div>伏望陛下密诏郭逵等，候至二广，熟计攻守利害，速具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159526_comment'></div>可往则往，如不可往，则令别图去就，以全王师之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159526_comment'></div>海峤阻远，恐难责其固必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159526_comment'></div>臣又窃闻秦陇之外，数年用兵，鮨取熙河等五州，别立一路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159526_comment'></div>辟地进境，开拓故疆，诚为国朝美事，足光史册也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159526_comment'></div>然而远近共传，当时杀戮人命，不可胜计，费耗财用，莫知纪极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159526_comment'></div>是皆主事者公为欺罔，不以实数上奏，致陛下无由得闻而进止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159526_comment'></div>今既立成部分，建置官属，屯兵守御，各有定制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159526_comment'></div>即须所得之地，所出之物，以供赡一路，自能取足，不假外求，然后可为长远之利，遂成开拓之益，则向者人命不为枉杀，财用不为虚费也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159526_comment'></div>奈何罢兵后，唯闻朝廷自京师辇运金帛，监司从内地支拨粮草，增添转遽，递铺奔走，不绝于道，滔滔而去，尚云不足！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159526_comment'></div>一二年来，又云彼中米麦每㪷计钱四五百文，贱亦不减三百以上，公私皇皇汲汲，日忧不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159526_comment'></div>若常如此，则不唯枉杀虚费，而又自此国家府库如何供亿，民间物力如何出办，遂使官私俱困，得之何用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159526_comment'></div>况陜西乏用，即今上下穷窘已甚，事茍得实，臣窃忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159526_comment'></div>伏愿陛下亲选无所畏惮公忠臣寮，不与其时用事人为党者，往彼按视土地可耕否，所收物货足用否，人情可安否，久远可守否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159526_comment'></div>俟得其实，然后委二府会议，方见经久利害如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159526_comment'></div>若不审行考校，但务竭力劳费，臣谓末等之家有十金之产者，且犹未肯如是，况乎为天下之计哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159526_comment'></div>惟陛下深切留意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159526_comment'></div>唐宣宗朝，北方亦曾自举十数州内附，未尝少加攻取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159526_comment'></div>既而供馈阙乏，终却叛去，唐亦不复顾藉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159526_comment'></div>更乞略赐检详，亦可以为證矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159526_comment'></div>臣又窃闻代北之地，狄人妄有争占，意在先发，殊无义理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159526_comment'></div>朝廷以其倔强难制，遂欲尽与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159526_comment'></div>此说传播甚盛，然终未知虚的。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159526_comment'></div>万一是的，则闻者莫不忧骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159526_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159526_comment'></div>盖夷狄贪婪，后患弥大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159526_comment'></div>彼曲我直，事甚明白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159526_comment'></div>且宜以理辨析，未易可许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159526_comment'></div>昔赵王欲赂强秦六城而虞卿不从，东胡欲求匈奴瓯脱而冒顿勿与，观其简册，足为龟炮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159526_comment'></div>愿陛下取此二说，以今疆事反覆参校始末轻重，与二府议定决然利害，奏禀而后行，此须特出宸断也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159526_comment'></div>臣又窃闻累年新法所行之事，条目甚多，陛下近已深见为害，但虚怀隐忍，未即更张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159526_comment'></div>此诚大得为君之道，从容优裕而不欲迫急也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159526_comment'></div>然所谓为害者，皆害及天下之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159526_comment'></div>被害既久，则岂尚容舒缓哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159526_comment'></div>度今事势正如解倒垂之急，唯恐解之不速也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159526_comment'></div>亦如人之感疾，疾深则难愈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159526_comment'></div>木之受蠹，蠹深则难补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159526_comment'></div>惟陛下所见害事既明，芽檗已著者，宜早图之，必无太早之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159526_comment'></div>更或稍缓，则遂成疾蠹深患，朝廷益难奠枕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159526_comment'></div>况天下不以贤愚，共知陛下始欲讲求大治，比迹唐虞，前代帝王用心非所能及，而不意为人所误至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159526_comment'></div>事皆成趎，究其端由，实非陛下之失，唯是众口共责为谋者，恨不食其肉焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159526_comment'></div>今圣情既已开悟，稔知其非，而犹隐忍护惜，不速更张，却恐遂玷圣德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159526_comment'></div>臣更愿陛下于左右臣僚中，不以职位高下，常视其反覆狡狯者疏之，纯良方正者与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159526_comment'></div>反覆狡狯者，虽有癚才强辨可以惑人，其如自取名位及援引亲旧，结成朋党，互相保庇，表里胶固，牢不可破，如此之类者，岂可置之左右而任之以事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159526_comment'></div>盖本无一定之志，不癴不仁，不畏不义，不见利不劝，必无忠尽悫实，安肯乃心于国家也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159526_comment'></div>纯良方正者，才辨诚有不及狡猾之人，然其心不二，持守坚笃，中立不倚，傍无朋比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159526_comment'></div>用之则直道而进，舍之则奉身而退，不为利回，不为义疚，忠亮之节，至死不移，不肯欺昧朝廷，自求多福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159526_comment'></div>如此等人，终无妄误，必能为国家立事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159526_comment'></div>假有未能立事者，亦不为害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159526_comment'></div>陛下临御既久，当尽照见，固难上逃圣炮，此尤宜常挂宸念，恐非须臾可忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159526_comment'></div>缘误用一二癚人，则展转援致，连茹而进，分布中外，大为朝廷之害，卒难救整。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159526_comment'></div>唐文宗所谓破河北贼易，破朝廷朋党难者，正为此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159526_comment'></div>天子无职事，唯辨别大臣邪正而进退之，此其职也，切乞谨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159526_comment'></div>臣狂瞽之说，实有爱君忧国之心，固无他志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159526_comment'></div>伏乞俯赐听纳，早赐裁处，不胜宗社生灵之幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1159526_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年6月</a>　本月因征讨安南，上疏建言。作品：《论蛮獠侵犯乞诏诸道以宽民为务奏》<div id='poem_1159527' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159527' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159527?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论蛮獠侵犯乞诏诸道以宽民为务奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁九年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159527")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159527_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159527'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159527'>臣退伏草茅，不预人事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159527_comment'></div>近者窃闻蠢尔蛮獠，犯我疆封，二广致灾，五岭严备，虽为手足之患，谅烦宵旰之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159527_comment'></div>然而命将得人，出师有日，上禀宸算，必成武功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159527_comment'></div>臣又窃闻淮南累岁尤为荒䭑，流亡饿殍，赈济难周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159527_comment'></div>今骤起数万之徒，间由诸路而往，兵马所到，粮草须办，监提守宰，唯务供军，府库仓箱，殆难足用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159527_comment'></div>既各求于集事，恐必致于扰民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159527_comment'></div>又有按察之官，继行督责之令，上下逼迫，公私煎熬，人心不宁，实可矜恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159527_comment'></div>臣又窃闻南方乡村城郭，重砯逋欠官司钱物，其数浩遆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159527_comment'></div>若监司州县又相迫催理，仍与此时赡军所费一并取足，则民不堪命，无以为生，啸聚惊骚，或难禁戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159527_comment'></div>陛下天赋仁圣，累降宽恤之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159527_comment'></div>其如所在阙用，出于无可奈何，须至侵渔，方能济集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159527_comment'></div>而又官吏各思一时茍免罪责，不暇为国家忧及后患而为长久之计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159527_comment'></div>臣又窃闻诸处兴修水利之类，役人甚众，多或至于一二十万，此伤耗民财，事亦不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159527_comment'></div>伏愿陛下深诏有司，并下诸道，以宽民为务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159527_comment'></div>凡所逋欠，可蠲者与蠲放，理难蠲放者多分料次，且令迤逦输纳，及权罢诸般兴作，全养民力，一意专以破贼为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159527_comment'></div>俟岭南宁息，岁时稍丰，然后别上图议，以称朝廷有为之心，固亦未晚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159527_comment'></div>臣杜门谢事，祗如聋瞽，但时得于四方之人传闻者，今录以上奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159527_comment'></div>茍有妄说，惟陛下恕其愚而怜其心，以来众正之路。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1159527_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　本年陈襄有来书问候。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='0e59dd21feac451db5df036443277816_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0e59dd21feac451db5df036443277816");'><span id='0e59dd21feac451db5df036443277816_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1083')">1078-1083年</a>，75-80岁</div><div id='0e59dd21feac451db5df036443277816' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年4月22日</a>　宗谔封豫章郡王，请范祖禹代回宗谔书。作品：《代富公回豫章郡王状》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年9月14日</a>　吕公著知枢密院，有书贺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　与文彦博、司马光。祖无择等在洛阳九人组成真率会，洛阳人谓之“九老”。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年10月</a>　本月太皇太后驾崩。程颐来书，言仁宗陵墓之弊，商议太皇太后合祔昭陵。有答。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年3月</a>　三月十一日，陈襄卒。托程颐上疏神宗皇帝，论永昭陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>　邵伯温除父丧，拜入门下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年闰9月26日</a>　因定策之功进司徒，字绍京为閤门祇候。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年</a>　在洛阳，深居简出。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年1月10日</a>　邀请文彦博、司马光等十三人为“洛阳耆英会”，赋诗饮酒相乐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　居洛阳。书座屏“守口如瓶，防意如城”八字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　本年上疏，论治乱，以为君子小人为治乱之本。作品：《论治乱之要疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（疏参《宋名臣奏议》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1159528' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159528' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159528?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论治乱之要疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰六年闰六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159528")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159528_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159528'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159528'>臣闻自古致天下治与乱者，大纲不出谀佞、谠直之人二端而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159528_comment'></div>谀佞者进，人主不闻有过，惟恶是为，所以致乱也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159528_comment'></div>谠直者进，则人主日有开益，惟善是从，所以致治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159528_comment'></div>此乃人主致治乱之大略焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159528_comment'></div>臣自离朝廷，退居林下，时亦仰知朝政所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159528_comment'></div>大率谀佞者竞进，谠直者多处于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159528_comment'></div>虽有在朝者，盖恐触忤癚佞，亦皆结舌不敢有所开陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159528_comment'></div>又闻近日中外或有事绪上挠圣怀，而忠义之士，但仰屋窃叹，不见有闻于上，致陛下不得知而更张之，此实非朝廷之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159528_comment'></div>惟愿陛下开忠正之路，杜群枉之门，讲求善政，变祸为福，俾天下受赐，坐致太平，此老臣有望于陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159528_comment'></div>其间事目甚多，亦不敢妄有条列，但举其大要，惟圣君留神而择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159528_comment'></div>不尔，即恐浸渍渐深，祸乱将至，则于时益烦宵旰之忧而亦无所济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159528_comment'></div>老臣犬马区区之志，略陈其端，伏望圣慈无少忽而深思之、力行之，乃天下之幸，宗社之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159528_comment'></div>臣窃观大凡臣僚上封论事，其间甚有事沽激取虚名者，亦有希利禄求实欲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159528_comment'></div>臣今年整八十，可谓老矣，近日尤觉衰鑓，举动须人扶策，家居坐卧，日与死迫，癋已致政十有馀年，固非事沽激希利禄之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159528_comment'></div>惟是忧国爱君之心愈深愈切，所以不量僭越，特有此奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159528_comment'></div>惟陛下少加省察，思而行之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1159528_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年春</a>　本年春，条陈时政得失以待用，交之付子绍庭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年5月</a>　有大星陨落所居还政堂；登天光台，焚香祭拜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年闰6月22日</a>　本日卒，年八十。赠太尉，谥号文忠。子绍庭上遗奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年闰6月22日</a>　卒后程颢、范纯仁、文彦博有祭文、哀辞，程颐有吊唁书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年7月23日</a>　子绍京卒，年三十七。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年7月</a>　范纯仁为富弼作行状。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年11月19日</a>　本日与其子绍京同葬河南府河南县金谷乡南张里。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
泰州（海陵）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='91cc9b65f3f649818c3c0bc15cfbfe9b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("91cc9b65f3f649818c3c0bc15cfbfe9b");'><span id='91cc9b65f3f649818c3c0bc15cfbfe9b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1022&endYear=1023')">1022-1023年</a>，19-20岁</div><div id='91cc9b65f3f649818c3c0bc15cfbfe9b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1022&endYear=1022')">1022年2月</a>　父富言迁官屯田员外郎，出监海陵，随行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>　居海陵，开始结识范仲淹，时范氏监泰州西溪镇盐仓。<br /></div>

-----title
商丘（睢阳）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='519070cd82d14d1e8aa9b50622a1a55a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("519070cd82d14d1e8aa9b50622a1a55a");'><span id='519070cd82d14d1e8aa9b50622a1a55a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1026')">1024-1026年</a>，21-23岁</div><div id='519070cd82d14d1e8aa9b50622a1a55a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年11月</a>　父富言移官山西。富弼在睢阳习学，与嵇颖游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1026')">1025-1026年</a>　居商丘。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f9bd39b0bc4b4443896656b094ff2ea7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f9bd39b0bc4b4443896656b094ff2ea7");'><span id='f9bd39b0bc4b4443896656b094ff2ea7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>，68岁</div><div id='f9bd39b0bc4b4443896656b094ff2ea7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年8月26日</a>　时张方平判南京御史台，过南京见之，语及王安石。<br /></div>

-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='863446009e2f4b53bd958a1f2e0ef871_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("863446009e2f4b53bd958a1f2e0ef871");'><span id='863446009e2f4b53bd958a1f2e0ef871_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1030')">1027-1030年</a>，24-27岁</div><div id='863446009e2f4b53bd958a1f2e0ef871' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年</a>　春，赴京师试礼部不中。晏殊知应天府，兴办学校，招范仲淹等生徒就学。八月，晏殊出任御史中臣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年12月</a>　本年冬，范仲淹任秘阁校理。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年闰2月</a>　富弼西归，范仲淹劝其试制科。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　范仲淹推荐富弼于王曾，晏殊许其女妻之。富弼与王、晏当与本年相识。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年11月</a>　在汴京。参加制举考试，上策论。富弼等十人词理皆优，仁宗皇帝命复校之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　在汴京。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　在汴京。晏殊知贡举。欧阳修、田况、蔡襄、石介同登科。在京师与欧阳修往来较多。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年6月</a>　在汴京，召试制科。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年7月26日</a>　以茂材异等中第，授监丞，知河南府长水县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年9月</a>　用丞相李迪荐辟，签书河阳（河南孟州）节度判官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　本年父亲富言知万州，弟弟富奭随行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2b291ea2373647f69d7ff3a59a9285b0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2b291ea2373647f69d7ff3a59a9285b0");'><span id='2b291ea2373647f69d7ff3a59a9285b0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>，30岁</div><div id='2b291ea2373647f69d7ff3a59a9285b0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年12月</a>　十二月后已经除丧，至京师，上表，不报。作品：《论废嫡后逐臣表》<div id='poem_1159471' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159471' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159471?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论废嫡后逐谏臣奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（明道二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159471")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159471_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159471'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159471'>臣闻右司谏、秘阁校理范仲淹，以上章谏废后事贬睦州通判，仍差人押出门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159471_comment'></div>臣不胜惊骇，伏恐陛下行于仓卒，未熟思虑，辄敢冒天威、犯斧钺，一陈愚恳，惟陛下裁察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159471_comment'></div>皇后自居中宫，不闻有过，陛下忽然废斥，物议腾踊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159471_comment'></div>自太祖、太宗、真宗，抚国凡七十年，未尝有此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159471_comment'></div>陛下为人子孙，不能遵祖考之训，而遂有废后之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159471_comment'></div>治家而尚不以道，奈天下何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159471_comment'></div>仲淹为谏官，所以极谏者，乃其职也，陛下何故罪之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159471_comment'></div>假使所谏不当，犹须含忍以招谏诤，况仲淹所谏，大惬亿万人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159471_comment'></div>陛下又纵私忿，不顾公议，取笑四方，臣甚为陛下不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159471_comment'></div>昔庄宪临朝，陛下受制，事体大弱，而庄宪不敢行武后故事者，盖赖一二忠臣救护，使庄宪不得纵其欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159471_comment'></div>陛下可以保其位，实忠臣之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159471_comment'></div>今陛下始获暂安，遂忘旧日忠臣，罗织其罪而谴逐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159471_comment'></div>陛下以万乘之尊，谓废一妇人，甚为小事，然所损之体则极大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159471_comment'></div>夫废后谓之家事，而不听外臣者，此唐奸臣许敬宗、李世绩谄佞之辞，陛下何足取法？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159471_comment'></div>陛下必欲废后，但可不纳所谏，何必加责，以重己过！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159471_comment'></div>今匹庶之家，或出妻，亦须告父母，父母许，然后敢出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159471_comment'></div>今陛下贵为天子，庄宪、庄懿山陵始毕，坟土未乾，便以色欲之心，废黜后氏而不告宗庙，是不敬父母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159471_comment'></div>今陛下举一事而获二过于天下，废无罪之后一也，逐忠臣二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159471_comment'></div>此二者，皆非太平之世所行，臣实痛惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159471_comment'></div>庄宪太后临朝，以刘从德死，恩典太重，台谏曹修古等四人连名上章极谏，庄宪大怒，陛下不得已，遂贬此四人，然心甚惜其去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159471_comment'></div>庄宪才往，陛下立行召命，优与恩奖，复处宪省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159471_comment'></div>修古虽死，厚加赠典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159471_comment'></div>如此者，盖陛下怜其忠鲠，不避夫祸难尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159471_comment'></div>今仲淹所谏，又甚于修古等所陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159471_comment'></div>修古等追用而仲淹黜弃，陛下何所见前后之异也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159471_comment'></div>况仲淹以忠直不挠，庄宪时论冬仗事，大正君臣之分，陛下以此自擢用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159471_comment'></div>既居谏列，或闻累曾宣谕，使小大之事必谏，无得有隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159471_comment'></div>是陛下欲闻过失，虽古先圣哲之主，亦无以过此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159471_comment'></div>今仲淹闻过遂谏，上副宣谕之意，而反及于祸，是陛下诱而陷之，不知自今后何以使臣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159471_comment'></div>虽日加宣谕，谏臣以仲淹为戒，必不信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159471_comment'></div>谏臣不谏，大非朝廷之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159471_comment'></div>今百执事所为，皆一司一局，虽常才者皆能干之，是易为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159471_comment'></div>如仲淹者，乃为臣之难能者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159471_comment'></div>今干一司一局者，皆坐取迁陟，立居显要，而仲淹不惜性命，为陛下论事，而远徙外郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159471_comment'></div>臣恐百辟以此皆务为易者，而不为难者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159471_comment'></div>陛下一旦有难为之事，不知何人为陛下为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159471_comment'></div>居谏官者，务要讦直，乃号称职，依违者旷职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159471_comment'></div>今循默者已居显要，而讦直者尚居散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159471_comment'></div>茍如是，不若废谏官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159471_comment'></div>如不欲废，即循默者可黜，讦直者可用，请陛下急图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159471_comment'></div>今天下凶歉，盗贼如麻，国用空虚，人心惶扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159471_comment'></div>奸雄观此，已有窥觎之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159471_comment'></div>陛下当兢兢惕惕，宵衣旰食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159471_comment'></div>日与臣寮讲论安天下之计，犹恐不及，而乃自作弗靖，废嫡后、逐谏臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159471_comment'></div>使此丑声闻于四方，知陛下不纳谏臣，朝政不举，则奸雄益喜，以谓中外皆乱，事势相符，必有变事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159471_comment'></div>臣一念至此，心寒骨颤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159471_comment'></div>此自然之兆，固非臣之臆说也，望陛下审思之，明察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159471_comment'></div>废后已行，虽未能悔过，臣愿陛下急且追还仲淹，复其谏职，减二过之一，庶乎谏路不绝，朝纲复振，使奸雄不能窥陛下浅深，此社稷之庆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159471_comment'></div>臣近免父丧赴阙，途中闻此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159471_comment'></div>今至京师，未及陛见，乃忘出位之责，而昧死有闻于陛下者，臣实不惜一仲淹，盖惜陛下所举措尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1159471_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6f4b3a3901b140b5945c77b3ed934b7e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6f4b3a3901b140b5945c77b3ed934b7e");'><span id='6f4b3a3901b140b5945c77b3ed934b7e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>，34岁</div><div id='6f4b3a3901b140b5945c77b3ed934b7e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年4月5日</a>　回京师，召试馆职。仁宗特命试以策论，后成为惯例。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　授太子中允、直集贤院。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c6ac49b8217d455ebc1947937699362d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c6ac49b8217d455ebc1947937699362d");'><span id='c6ac49b8217d455ebc1947937699362d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1042')">1039-1042年</a>，36-39岁</div><div id='c6ac49b8217d455ebc1947937699362d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年闰12月23日</a>　本日召为开封府推官，知谏院。作品：《乞诏陕西等路奏举才武奏》<div id='poem_1159473' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159473' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159473?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞诏陕西等路奏举才武奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝元二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年闰12月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159473")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159473_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159473'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159473'>臣伏睹载籍，自古取士，无如本朝路狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159473_comment'></div>三代以往，不复纪列，两汉而下，历南北朝及隋唐十馀代，取士之法，各有科条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159473_comment'></div>大率如贤良、孝廉、孝弟力田、明经、秀才、进士，唐又添制举五十馀科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159473_comment'></div>此外又许藩镇辟召及诸色人荐举，亦许自荐拜官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159473_comment'></div>历代求人，唯务广博，所以天下怀才抱器之士，无不牢笼收揽，尽为朝廷之所用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159473_comment'></div>国家取人，唯有进士、明经二科，虽近设制举，亦又取人不多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159473_comment'></div>是三者，大抵只考文辞念诵而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159473_comment'></div>天下之士，有大才大行而赋性不能为文辞就举试者，率皆遗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159473_comment'></div>臣窃思近年数榜以来放及第者，如河北、河东、陕西，此三路之人所得绝少者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159473_comment'></div>盖此处人物禀性质鲁，不能为文辞、中程试，故皆老于科场，至死不能得一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159473_comment'></div>岂三路之人独不乐富贵哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159473_comment'></div>盖求之而不得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159473_comment'></div>今纵有稍在显官者，亦不过三五人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159473_comment'></div>此数路之人虽不能为文辞，若其大才大行及强悍奸雄，则诸路不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159473_comment'></div>向时天下无事，则此等人或在场屋，或在农亩，或在商贾，或在僧道，屈伏不能有所为，但怨望思乱而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159473_comment'></div>今元昊寇边，西陲用武，覆军杀将，中外震恐，兵寡粮匮，调发无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159473_comment'></div>当是之时，乃此等人踊跃快意，皆欲助贼为患，或更有盗贼屯聚，则为之倡首，惊劫州县，自图富贵之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159473_comment'></div>其间忠义者，尚思因时驻屯，而愿为朝廷之用者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159473_comment'></div>然朝廷至今未悟，不加搜访，臣恐为他人所得，则中国处处皆为敌国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159473_comment'></div>臣伏见汉高祖作歌，曰「安得猛士兮守四方」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159473_comment'></div>武帝又亲作诏，令州郡察吏民，举可为将相及使绝域者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159473_comment'></div>唐高祖亦敕关内、河东诸州，召募勇敢，以讨吐蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159473_comment'></div>此皆前王所行而有济时用者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159473_comment'></div>臣又见朝廷向来所用之人，多至败事，虽切求人，未见可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159473_comment'></div>陛下勿谓在官皆人杰，而民间无复有人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159473_comment'></div>臣欲乞条列名目，如临难不顾、勇敢绝伦、武足安边、才任将帅、武艺超众、智谋宏远并可使绝域之类，列十馀条，特降手诏，下陕西、河北、河东、京东、京西路转运使副、提点刑狱及诸州长吏，仰依上项名目，察访举奏，不拘人物，不限人数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159473_comment'></div>能作文字者，即试以策问，勿限字数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159473_comment'></div>不能为文者，但令直说事状，或口陈方略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159473_comment'></div>亦许诣阙自荐，仍各量给装钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159473_comment'></div>如审知可用，即文武资中，随其所欲，量高下补授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159473_comment'></div>如此，必然得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159473_comment'></div>伏缘太平已久，武人在显位者或以恩泽进，或以年劳升，自馀门荫杂调，皆是常人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159473_comment'></div>不闻自孤寒中，才武擢用，臣所以谓非常人多在民间，自是不求，或求之不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159473_comment'></div>若果行此，必非虚设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159473_comment'></div>今岁或有贡举，兼之不妨，若贡举权罢，独行此诏，亦不失人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1159473_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年1月</a>　在京师。上奏不纳。作品：《论正旦日食请罢晏奏》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　在京师。曾言魏昭炳、郑守忠、高化不可用，不纳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年2月2日</a>　批评宋庠严守备于潼关之请。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年2月4日</a>　上罢王守忠之任奏，不纳。作品：《乞罢内侍王守忠钤辖之任奏》<div id='poem_1159476' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159476' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159476?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢内侍王守忠钤辖之任奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159476")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159476_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159476'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159476'>唐代之衰，始疑将帅，遂以内臣监军，取败非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159476_comment'></div>今守忠为都钤辖，与监军何异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159476_comment'></div>昨用夏守赟，已失人望，愿罢守忠勿遣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1159476_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年2月</a>　上奏一则，从之。作品：《乞令宰相兼枢密使奏》<div id='poem_1159477' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159477' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159477?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞令宰相兼枢密使奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159477")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159477_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159477'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159477'>臣伏见自来兵机公事，全委密院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159477_comment'></div>今边鄙多故，不同往时，若无更张，必有败阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159477_comment'></div>况事干治乱，执政岂可不知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159477_comment'></div>文武二途，自古一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159477_comment'></div>臣窃观周史，宰相魏仁浦曾兼枢密使，国初范质、王溥亦以宰相参知枢密院事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159477_comment'></div>臣今欲乞依故事，亦令宰相兼枢密使，所贵同心协力，各无猜嫌，共议安边，必能集事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1159477_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年2月15日</a>　本日，朝廷听从富弼建议，厚赏西夏首领。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年2月21日</a>　本日，朝廷听从富弼建议，解除越职言事之禁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年3月24日</a>　本日，朝廷听从富弼建议，诏诸路荐举有才任将帅者。。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年4月3日</a>　本日，改任监铁判官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年4月</a>　为刘平辩诬，弹劾中官卢守勤等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年10月</a>　入辞便殿，上防寇奏，不报。作品：《乞东南诸郡募兵以防寇盗奏》<div id='poem_1159478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞东南诸郡募兵以防寇盗奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159478")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159478'>臣闻天下大器也，非法制网罗不可以守矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159478_comment'></div>生民重畜也，非智力控御不可以保矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159478_comment'></div>是故先王兢兢业业，日谨一日，唯恐失大器而丧重畜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159478_comment'></div>臣伏见西戎僭叛，屡寇边境，本道不足以支，朝廷悉发京东、京西、淮南、江南、荆湖南北、两浙、福建、广南东西凡十一道兵以屯关中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159478_comment'></div>十一道兵素寡弱，又罹此调发，故关中得之未足以充，而十一道之兵已尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159478_comment'></div>朝廷独念京东邻河朔，京西次关陕，此二道不可以无备，遂遣使阅乡民，俾习武以代军兵，东南九道则不之省，臣未谕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159478_comment'></div>伏思朝廷用度，如军食、币帛、茶盐、泉货、金铜、铅银以至羽毛、胶漆、尽出此九道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159478_comment'></div>朝廷所以能安然理天下而不匮者，得此九道供亿使之然尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159478_comment'></div>此九道者，朝廷所仰给也，固宜保守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159478_comment'></div>今尽取其兵，是不加保守，一日乘虚盗起，梗其津要，则京师无故而坐困矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159478_comment'></div>凡奸贼好窥觊者，无世不有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159478_comment'></div>今西鄙用兵，天下兵与将皆集于西方，力必不能及他道，则就无备而作焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159478_comment'></div>以臣观此九道州军，或一豪杰率数十夫，伺州官朔望行香毕集，持锄䥳白梃，群呼奋击，可尽杀之，谁复御者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159478_comment'></div>然后开府库，复劫取豪家物，散施召募，必应者如云，一日可得千计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159478_comment'></div>鼓行而前，处处无兵，又城垒不修，诸郡县镇所至必陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159478_comment'></div>俟奏至朝廷，即时发兵，亦不减三两月方至，则其徒必及万数，何可破邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159478_comment'></div>臣又虑陛下以谓巨寇必不能猝至，臣不敢远稽前古，略引隋唐以来东南为寇者以明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159478_comment'></div>隋大业年中，刘元进起馀杭，朱燮、管崇起吴，各拥数十万，寇江浙诸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159478_comment'></div>朱粲起谯郡，拥兵数十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159478_comment'></div>寇宏起鄱阳，萧铣起罗县，各众数万，攻陷诸郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159478_comment'></div>唐咸通年中，桂林戍卒五百人杀其将，以判官庞勋为都头，剽掠湘、潭，后陷徐、宿等州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159478_comment'></div>又乾符年中，海贼王郢、江贼柳彦章，各聚徒数万馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159478_comment'></div>光化年中，鲁景仁起连州，黄岫起桂阳，沈行收起邵阳，各拥兵万馀，攻本郡邑，杀戮守长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159478_comment'></div>其甚盛者，则江西钟傅、广南刘隐、湖南马商、福建王潮，皆割据焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159478_comment'></div>臣谓东南九道，负山阻水，为寇者足以倔强，故自古为寇渊薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159478_comment'></div>唯王者能镇抚之，则寇不能生于其间，不然则乱之必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159478_comment'></div>今九道大小一百三十馀郡，若每郡皆宿兵，固不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159478_comment'></div>臣欲乞于九道中，择要害约十馀郡，如泗、扬、升、洪、吉、潭、荆、桂、广、福、杭、越之类，按地里相去均者，于本处募兵，大郡五千，小郡三二千，以多补少，不过四五万人，以东南百三十郡之富，岂不能赡养哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159478_comment'></div>训为精兵，勿复差役，每郡置二督护专领之，每道别置一都护经略之，九道又置一总管者居中以节制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159478_comment'></div>如此，则欲为寇者知朝廷有备，岂不顾惮耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159478_comment'></div>设有盗起，则发兵有所，济师有地，乘其未甚炽而扑灭之，不为难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159478_comment'></div>臣前所谓天下生民宜网罗而控制之者，以此道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159478_comment'></div>臣伏念京东、京西，虽置乡兵，而军兵绝寡，亦未见久安之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159478_comment'></div>夫乡兵无营垒，散处村堡，又各持兵仗，其部伍上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159478_comment'></div>终不得如军兵之肃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159478_comment'></div>或因饥馑为奸桀倡之，安能使必不为盗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159478_comment'></div>又宜得军兵两相制御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159478_comment'></div>况山东自古尤多寇盗，隋大业年中韩进、甄宝起济北，张金称起清河，窦建德、格谦、孙宣雅起渤海，孟襄、杜伏威起齐，逐郡各拥众十馀万人，劫掠诸郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159478_comment'></div>唐乾符中，王仙芝起濮州，聚众亦十馀万，转攻河南十五郡，以至黄巢起宛朐，拥众百万，陷覆两京，横行天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159478_comment'></div>虽然，观其初起草莽，盖亦甚微，当时制御失策，遂至滋蔓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159478_comment'></div>今亦乞择要害数郡，募兵立帅，如东南之制，则可无虞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159478_comment'></div>议者或谓财用不足，恐难成此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159478_comment'></div>夫以天下安全之业，尚患财窘而不能立久长之策，不幸小有寇聚，则如之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159478_comment'></div>伏惟陛下以宗社为忧，以生民为念，裁制私欲，损节横费，则数万之众，不日可募，此无疆之基也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1159478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年5月</a>　改官右正言、知制诰，纠察在京刑狱。赐三品服。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　本年还上革科举法令奏。作品：《乞革科举之法令牧守监司举奏》<div id='poem_1159479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159479?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞革科举之法令牧守监司举士奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159479")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159479'>臣伏以取士之道，为国家之大务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159479_comment'></div>三代、两汉，专求行实，是以风俗淳厚，百职修举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159479_comment'></div>隋唐之际，纯用文辞，以篇赋相高，以声誉相尚，公卿将相于是乎出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159479_comment'></div>国朝沿隋唐之制，以进士取人，祇采辞华，不求行实；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159479_comment'></div>虽间设制举，然大率亦以章句为务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159479_comment'></div>是以择之弥谨，而失之愈疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159479_comment'></div>且以陛下临御以来计之，积二十年所得，不减三千馀人，其间确然为名公巨贤者无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159479_comment'></div>近日窃见朝廷欲选一二良吏而终未能得，其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159479_comment'></div>盖入仕之初，但取空文，不求实才实行之所致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159479_comment'></div>今天下多事，边鄙未宁，若不求人，将何以济？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159479_comment'></div>求人之本，唯科场最大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159479_comment'></div>科场之法，行之已久，尽革则骇众，不革则乏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159479_comment'></div>臣欲今后科场考试，以策论为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159479_comment'></div>校度所放人数，且取其半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159479_comment'></div>馀半诏天下诸州，于境内搜访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159479_comment'></div>土著之人，自来为乡党所推，或德行纯备，或志节方劲，或学识该敏，或智略详明，或有才可以治民，或知兵可以御敌，如此之类者，仰逐州官吏同共察访，委实应得上项条目，即具名闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159479_comment'></div>仍以州郡大小限其人数，令长吏以礼津遣，年终集于都下，朝廷再加较试，量高下擢用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159479_comment'></div>若举荐不当，明行降黜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159479_comment'></div>或所举得人，则优与酬赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159479_comment'></div>昔汉尚书令左雄建明孝廉之法，颁下郡国，是时济阴太守胡广等十馀人，皆坐谬举黜免，唯汝南陈蕃、颍川李膺、下邳陈球等三十馀人，得拜郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159479_comment'></div>自是牧守畏慄，莫敢轻举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159479_comment'></div>东汉得人之盛，唯此为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159479_comment'></div>伏惟陛下勉而行之，不数年当尽得天下实才实行之士萃于朝廷，缓急应用，百务俱理，又何患乏人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159479_comment'></div>必若行此，取士之数则不加，而得人之实则多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159479_comment'></div>至于明经选试，尤为无法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159479_comment'></div>乞今后不较字数，专以经中否为格，仍试时务策三道，以定高下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159479_comment'></div>每度所放人数，祇取其半，自然得人而不至冗矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1159479_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　本年梅尧臣在外任监湖州盐税途中有诗寄来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年1月27日</a>　本日，因契丹派遣人员索地，富弼担任接伴使。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='997aa4d8f8d84d9892d036c382cbc54c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("997aa4d8f8d84d9892d036c382cbc54c");'><span id='997aa4d8f8d84d9892d036c382cbc54c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>，39岁</div><div id='997aa4d8f8d84d9892d036c382cbc54c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年2月5日</a>　上奏论省试殿试长短。作品：《论省试殿试长短奏》<div id='poem_1159480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159480?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论省试殿试长短奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年2月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159480")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159480'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159480'>国家缘隋唐之制，设进士之科，采天下贤俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159480_comment'></div>虽至公之道过于隋唐，而得人之实或有未至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159480_comment'></div>自咸平、景德年后，条约渐密，然省试有三长，殿试有三短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159480_comment'></div>南省主文者四五人，皆两制宗匠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159480_comment'></div>又选馆阁有辞学者数人，以助主文考校；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159480_comment'></div>复有监守、巡察、糊名、誊录，上下相警，不能容毫釐之私，此一长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159480_comment'></div>又一日试诗、赋，一日试论，一日试策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159480_comment'></div>诗、赋可以见辞艺，策、论可以见才识，四方之士，得以尽其所蕴，此二长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159480_comment'></div>又贡院凡两月馀日研磨差次，必俟穷功悉力，然后榜出，此三长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159480_comment'></div>可谓至公至精矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159480_comment'></div>以此姓名高下，遂放及第，辞艺才识高者得高科，下者得下等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159480_comment'></div>高科者待以好爵，下等者归于常调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159480_comment'></div>朝廷既不失其实，举人又各足其志矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159480_comment'></div>洎至殿试，号为亲临，然所差考校之官，多不精慎，此一短也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159480_comment'></div>又只试诗、赋与论，并在一日，不能尽人之才，此二短也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159480_comment'></div>又考校不过十日，不暇研磨差次，匆匆而定，此三短也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159480_comment'></div>向之省试至公至精也，乃混淆而不复见，今舍其所长，用其所短者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159480_comment'></div>或云省试放榜则恩归有司，殿试放榜则恩由主上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159480_comment'></div>是尽弃取士之实而沽此虚名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159480_comment'></div>普天率土，岂有恩不出天子者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159480_comment'></div>况殿试非古，始于唐武后之初年尔，此安足为后世法？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159480_comment'></div>历代取士，悉委有司，独后汉文吏课笺奏而副之端门，亦未闻天子再试也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159480_comment'></div>往时无糊名、誊录之制，主文可以专取舍，遂有殿试以防主文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159480_comment'></div>今无以容其私，殿试复何为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159480_comment'></div>臣欲乞自今岁以后，只令南宫放榜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159480_comment'></div>必恐恩归有司，则请如天圣二年，令南宫考定高下，以混榜引于殿庭，依次唱名赐第，则与殿试同矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1159480_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年3月28日</a>　本日授礼部员外郎、枢密直学士，坚辞不受。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9a5121d2784d4120aa8cdc89c90dc208_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9a5121d2784d4120aa8cdc89c90dc208");'><span id='9a5121d2784d4120aa8cdc89c90dc208_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>，39岁</div><div id='9a5121d2784d4120aa8cdc89c90dc208' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年7月17日</a>　仁宗追用富弼建议，以宰相兼枢密使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年7月22日</a>　再次出使契丹，因诏书有误，面责吕夷简、晏殊。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年7月</a>　长子富绍庭出生。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='552c89aa7d9841da9d7588fdccff1750_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("552c89aa7d9841da9d7588fdccff1750");'><span id='552c89aa7d9841da9d7588fdccff1750_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1044')">1042-1044年</a>，39-41岁</div><div id='552c89aa7d9841da9d7588fdccff1750' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年9月25日</a>　回到京师，朝廷从晏殊建议，许称“纳”字。富弼没有料到。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年闰9月10日</a>　辞吏部郎中、枢密直学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年10月6日</a>　本日升迁翰林学士，不拜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年11月15日</a>　本日与范仲淹一起建议孙复为试校书郎、国子监直讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年3月22日</a>　本日除右谏议大夫、枢密副使。上章辞。时有足疾，居家疗养。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年3月27日</a>　改任资政殿学士兼翰林侍读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年4月2日</a>　上奏关于对待契丹使。作品：《不可待西使太过奏》<div id='poem_1159483' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159483' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159483?labeling=true' target='_blank'>不可待西使太过奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年4月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159483")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159483_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159483'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159483'>臣近者窃闻昊贼遣其伪六宅使贺从勉赍书到阙，欲议通好，事颇秘密，臣不知审实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159483_comment'></div>但外人传说，昊贼来书，未肯称臣，别图位号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159483_comment'></div>兼臣昨在西京，闲居养疾，窃见传宣下河西一路州军，排备祗候西使，次第甚盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159483_comment'></div>又令逐州通判就驿相看，置酒管领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159483_comment'></div>臣甚忧事体太过，必恐下面难为处置，有失中国制驭夷狄之术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159483_comment'></div>臣又窃闻西使之来，非自然之意，盖契丹特遣使往河西，教之令来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159483_comment'></div>既是元昊禀畏契丹，使来贡奉，元昊不敢不从，即不假匆忙，可且持重与之商议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159483_comment'></div>纵时下未合，必有后图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159483_comment'></div>今来请和，既不由元昊，使人岂能专其可否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159483_comment'></div>以此思之，朝廷待西使不必过当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159483_comment'></div>大凡措置机事，在乎制之于初，初若失宜，后难救应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159483_comment'></div>臣又今日窃闻西使入见，赐与甚多，既许人使伪官之称，则元昊所图，势难止遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159483_comment'></div>茍一一遂其所欲，臣不知向去事体如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159483_comment'></div>况臣去年两使北庭，所议西事甚是分明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159483_comment'></div>臣前后邀勒度数颇多，不能一一记忆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159483_comment'></div>臣今省得再去时，与馆伴刘六符所说一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159483_comment'></div>臣谓六符云：「北朝将来令元昊如何归附？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159483_comment'></div>须是却令依旧纳欸，不可令别有所望」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159483_comment'></div>六符云：「固是如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159483_comment'></div>况元昊自来称臣于南朝，今来更待望甚定，是须令纳欸称臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159483_comment'></div>况南朝与北朝书云，彼若翻然效顺，此必待之如初」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159483_comment'></div>臣今记得上项一节甚明，伏乞朝廷检会臣再奉使过日别录照对，方见的实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159483_comment'></div>向者所许北庭岁添金帛之数，盖为令他指挥西事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159483_comment'></div>初既不避张此名声，今来又却不依旧约，则是虚受前耻而不获后效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159483_comment'></div>甚可痛惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159483_comment'></div>此事朝廷须是广为思虑，何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159483_comment'></div>北狄元许却令称臣，今来自是朝廷过有许可，亦恐北狄意不欲，谓元昊于中国尚不肯称臣，于我岂肯甘分？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159483_comment'></div>则是因此致使北狄亦难制元昊，元昊亦自此所图愈大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159483_comment'></div>若北狄遣使以此来问，则朝廷何辞以对？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159483_comment'></div>又虑元昊若不称臣于朝廷，则北狄必曰，元昊本称臣于我，亦称臣于南朝，今元昊既于南朝不复称臣，渐为敌国，则是元昊与南朝等，惟我契丹独尊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159483_comment'></div>臣谓北狄因此益炽，必自喜名分暗定，异日稍有衅隙，缘此若有所求，则未知朝廷何以待之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159483_comment'></div>臣旦夕思此二事，将必有一焉，不可不深图，不可不早虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159483_comment'></div>愿朝廷且执北狄所约，更加裁择，不可容易过许，则不至别生后患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159483_comment'></div>臣又恐延州及京师干当事人且贪成功，不为国家思后来之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159483_comment'></div>伏乞陛下与两府臣寮深切计虑，必无后悔，然后从而行之，则天下之幸，宗社之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159483_comment'></div>臣不胜恳恳之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1159483_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年4月7日</a>　因韩琦、范仲淹为枢密副使，有奏。作品：《乞令韩琦范仲淹更任内外事奏》<div id='poem_1159482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159482?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞令韩琦范仲淹更任内外事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年4月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159482")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159482'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159482'>臣伏闻近降敕命，除陕西四路招讨经略使韩琦、范仲淹，并授枢密副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159482_comment'></div>仰认圣意，只从公论，不听谗毁，擢用孤远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159482_comment'></div>天下之人，皆谓朝廷进用大臣常如此日，则太平不难致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159482_comment'></div>然议者惟云进用大臣虽则美矣，其如西寇未殄，亦须藉才，若二人俱来，或恐阙事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159482_comment'></div>群论皆愿一名召来，使处内，一名就授枢副之命，且令在边，表里相应，事无不集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159482_comment'></div>以臣愚虑，亦谓群众所说甚得允当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159482_comment'></div>然近日或闻有异议者，谓枢密副使不可令带出外任，恐他时武官援此为例，深不稳便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159482_comment'></div>此乃横生所见，巧为其说，沮陛下独断之明，害天下至公之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159482_comment'></div>臣谓立此异议者，必知韩琦、范仲淹以西事方急，坚辞此职，既未肯从命而来，又不令带出外任，是欲惑君听，抑贤才，奸邪用心，一至于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159482_comment'></div>况先朝累曾有大臣带两府职任，应急出外，事毕还朝，不闻后来有武臣援以为例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159482_comment'></div>臣愿陛下无信异说，专采公论，一名召来，使处于内，一名就授枢副之职，且令在边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159482_comment'></div>或许二人一岁一更，均其劳逸，亦甚稳便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159482_comment'></div>内外协济，无善于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159482_comment'></div>臣旦夕来闻韩琦、范仲淹已有奏报，西事未了，恳辞恩命，朝廷乘此处分，深合事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159482_comment'></div>臣不胜恳恳激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1159482_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年4月2日</a>　应诏新除资政殿学士入班位。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年7月12日</a>　再授枢密副使，辞。要求补外，不许。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年8月13日</a>　正式受命为枢密副使。范仲淹为参知政事。尹洙有贺启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年9月</a>　受仁宗诏命，与范仲淹讨论当时急务，令主北事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年10月</a>　上捕盗寇奏。作品：《乞诸道置兵以备寇盗奏》《乞选任转运守令除盗贼奏》<div id='poem_1159485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞诸道置兵以备寇盗奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159485")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159485'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159485'>臣窃闻知金州、比部员外郎王茂先奏，九月十三日卯时，有群贼入州城，打开军资库、甲仗库，般运出衣甲物帛，散与贼众及贫民等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159485_comment'></div>知州以下只领当直兵士二十四人，斗敌不住，州官走出城外，任贼劫掠，直至未时以来，方始出城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159485_comment'></div>臣谓贼势转盛，深可忧虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159485_comment'></div>臣前岁曾陈备贼之策，正为今日之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159485_comment'></div>今来累有群贼白日入城，开军资等库，劫取衣甲物帛，散与贼党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159485_comment'></div>州中兵士不满三十人，州官散走，贼徒恣行劫杀，殊无畏惮，官司势不能制御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159485_comment'></div>臣前岁所陈，只是过为堤防万一或有此事，不意今来便至如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159485_comment'></div>小寇聚集，尚陵侮朝廷，臣决知自此后，更有大盗杀官吏，据州城，尽取官私财物，召募徒众，必千万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159485_comment'></div>且贼头称王称朕，与朝廷相抗，大劫财物，散施无涯，则贫民乐随矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159485_comment'></div>恣行劫杀，务要震恐，则小大胁从矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159485_comment'></div>朝廷赏必有限，罚必有条，不得如贼之使人乐随而胁从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159485_comment'></div>若诸处观望，奸雄相应而起，贼满天下，则大事去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159485_comment'></div>秦末、隋末、唐末，皆由此而乱，臣夙夜思念，实为寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159485_comment'></div>臣伏思西贼未叛以前，诸处虽有盗贼，未尝有敢杀戮官吏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159485_comment'></div>自四五年来，贼杀都巡检、县尉官者约五六十员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159485_comment'></div>又西贼未叛以前，诸处虽有盗贼，未尝敢入州城行劫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159485_comment'></div>自四五年来，贼入州县打劫者约三四十州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159485_comment'></div>向来入城，尚皆暮夜窃发，潜形来往，今则白日公行，擅开府库，其势日盛一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159485_comment'></div>自此以往，只有转炽，若不早为堤备，事未可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159485_comment'></div>臣前岁所上备贼之策，当时不曾施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159485_comment'></div>近日因两府奏事，论及淮南贼盗，陛下问臣前策，臣次日再录一本进呈讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159485_comment'></div>然臣策只是备兵聚东南九路及京东一路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159485_comment'></div>今据金州奏，在城只有兵士二十四人，显是无备，致盗生心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159485_comment'></div>今并京西一路亦于要害聚兵，为州郡声援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159485_comment'></div>今诸处贼盗已盛，方思设备，已失堤防，若又迁延，则无所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159485_comment'></div>伏乞速赐施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1159485_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1159497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159497?labeling=true'
