ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年8月</a>　本月王安石母丧，以书慰勉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年11月</a>　应韩琦之请，为其父撰《神道碑》。作品：《韩国华神道碑》<div id='poem_1159553' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159553' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159553?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋故太中大夫行右谏议大夫上柱国南阳县开国男食邑三百户赐紫金鱼袋赠开府仪同三司太师中书令兼尚书令魏国公韩公神道碑铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序嘉祐八年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159553")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159553_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159553'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159553'>丞相卫国公使以书来告曰：「我先人没于大中祥符四年春三月之甲申，葬于庆历五年春二月之己酉，虽论行有状，志圹有铭，载于史有传，施之幽显，不为无述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159553_comment'></div>然墓在吾里相州安阳县之新安村，有窆棺之碑存诸隧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159553_comment'></div>公雅与我游，又尝陪议军国于二府，知吾家为详，宜为我列先人事实刻于其上，以表于道，灿然使后世观之者曰，此有宋贤臣之墓，可信不惑，不待钩考而后见，则吾志毕矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159553_comment'></div>予曰：「诺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159553_comment'></div>按《春秋》，晋侯有子食韩原，其后遂以韩命氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159553_comment'></div>六卿裂晋自王，又有以韩国为氏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159553_comment'></div>子孙散适诸郡国，其在昌黎者最为著姓，公即昌黎之裔也，达者历世不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159553_comment'></div>远祖徙居深州之博野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159553_comment'></div>四代祖曰碍宾，事唐僖宗，为镇、冀、深、赵等州节度判官，检校太子左庶子，兼御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159553_comment'></div>时巢寇乱中原，其帅王景崇檄诸镇兵大破之，谋皆出于庶子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159553_comment'></div>庶子生二子，其季曰昌辞，于公为曾王父，终于真定府鼓城令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159553_comment'></div>鼓城生趚，为王父，少自力学，工为歌诗，与晋人李崧、徐台符深相善，名重一时，任广晋府永济令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159553_comment'></div>避乱，又徙居赵郡之赞皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159553_comment'></div>台符为作诗，哀其不达而终，其诗甚悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159553_comment'></div>崧乃以其弟之女妻其子构，即公之考妣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159553_comment'></div>考始居于相，以文章称，尤妙书奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159553_comment'></div>诸侯府争辟之，能致之者，即一府遂治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159553_comment'></div>尝宰贝州之清河，始至，与民约曰：「屈法扰人等事，吾断腕不为，惟惠利者为若力之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159553_comment'></div>民于是大说，然亦畏伏，丝毫不敢犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159553_comment'></div>历事周、晋二代，以世乱，亦不得进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159553_comment'></div>入宋，艺祖平南海，鮂选守臣，乃命知康州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159553_comment'></div>未几，以太子中允卒于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159553_comment'></div>公渐显，累赠工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159553_comment'></div>有子四人，公于次为第三，讳国华，字光弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159553_comment'></div>幼而警绝，乡举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159553_comment'></div>太宗初，一上中兴国二年甲科，授大理评事、通判泸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159553_comment'></div>代还，迁右赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159553_comment'></div>会诏与相帅择贤佐，改彰德军节度判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159553_comment'></div>凡从宦者，率以乡里为难，至则敛锋锷，一煦以恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159553_comment'></div>公时年尚少，处之气益劲，不为少损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159553_comment'></div>有民李氏者，怙富杀人，乃厚以贿州之上下，为汩其情，将不蜫于死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159553_comment'></div>公持之，尽抉其癚隐，李卒弃市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159553_comment'></div>由是诸豪惮之，砯足不敢动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159553_comment'></div>公每出，按辔俨然，未尝妄视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159553_comment'></div>里人每置酒，赌曰：有见其左右顾者，饮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159553_comment'></div>至罢去，竟不得饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159553_comment'></div>时国用方窘，半倚关赋，乃升秘书省著作郎、监上蔡税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159553_comment'></div>以监察御史召，弹击有眣角，珀然望高于台阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159553_comment'></div>属天子议复燕蓟，揣庭臣曰：「安得勇而善辞令者，为我谕高丽，出兵西攻契丹，以分其力，则吾事可不劳而集」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159553_comment'></div>既曰：「非韩某不可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159553_comment'></div>即假以太常少卿为使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159553_comment'></div>公驰舸至其国，其王负固，不时奉诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159553_comment'></div>公坐馆舍，遗王书，责以慢命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159553_comment'></div>且称「朝廷威德之盛，诸僭伪悉已擒灭，遂欲北取故疆以雪晋癴，而委王以方面者，其意不已重乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159553_comment'></div>王惟我中国是赖，可以得志，诸部虽暂勤而众，实王长世之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159553_comment'></div>今若不勉，天子怒，一日大兵东出，先诛不用命者，如决海灌爝火，王其无悔」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159553_comment'></div>王大恐，奔走率职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159553_comment'></div>明日，遣太相韩光、元辅赵抗领兵数万，度演江以侵契丹，且令光等率诸将诣馆门听令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159553_comment'></div>公待以陪臣礼，为指画方略，衔勒而慰遣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159553_comment'></div>师期未集，公又累与王书，奖激砻砺，使不得少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159553_comment'></div>复问曰：「深入攻之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159553_comment'></div>姑挑战也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159553_comment'></div>王报曰：「已深入矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159553_comment'></div>公得其肝胆，遂复命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159553_comment'></div>天子大喜，拜右拾遗、直史馆，面赐五品服章，兼判登闻院，入三司为开拆推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159553_comment'></div>公论开拆司主出纳三部文籍，置推官其名不正，宜更判事之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159553_comment'></div>寻诏改主判三司开拆司，迁左司谏，充盐铁判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159553_comment'></div>久之，契丹大将萧宁遣使叩雄州约和，州将刘福信之，以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159553_comment'></div>天子因思高丽功，立命公走雄州按其事，亦命代福作报书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159553_comment'></div>索其情伪，宁之意欲我先发，公固愿息兵以养民，然念国体不可屈，书十馀反，终不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159553_comment'></div>复意其谲而有谋，乃谢使者，急令备边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159553_comment'></div>还奏，天子又大喜，益爱其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159553_comment'></div>故事，凡曲燕，五品以下官非隶馆阁者不预。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159553_comment'></div>时燕侍臣于苑中，公以在盐铁例罢史局，不得入侍，天子特命直昭文馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159553_comment'></div>三司判官兼馆职自公始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159553_comment'></div>既又历判盐铁、度支、户部三勾院，改左计司判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159553_comment'></div>主计者嫌其守正不肯下，密谗于帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159553_comment'></div>帝雅信公，即日诏总判三勾，赐三品服章，仍令宰相召于政事堂谕旨，谗者大沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159553_comment'></div>公图报，益自奋，条三司不便事二十七上之，官民偕利，后无以易者，遂著为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1159553_comment'></div>俄出为京东转运副使，即拜峡路转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1159553_comment'></div>峡为险远一路，官俸薄，不可责以廉，公奏益之，至今峡中官德公不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1159553_comment'></div>真宗即位，入判大理寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1159553_comment'></div>自始登尚书秩至是凡五迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1159553_comment'></div>为职方郎中出知河阳，徙潞州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1159553_comment'></div>会契丹由梁门入寇河朔，分兵略太行，其锋甚锐，潞人恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1159553_comment'></div>公以精骑屯吴儿谷，扼其奔冲，贼遂不敢犯其境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1159553_comment'></div>又率本道粮以饷朔军，王师大济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1159553_comment'></div>帝嘉之，褒以玺书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1159553_comment'></div>景德初，契丹再寇澶渊，骤请修好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1159553_comment'></div>朝廷以其多变诈，使绝域者难其人，人亦惮其往，故首命公假秘书监为国信使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1159553_comment'></div>江南饥，又遣巡抚，专一道之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1159553_comment'></div>还朝，权开封府判官，出知曹州，拜太常少卿，徙泉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1159553_comment'></div>天子封太山，擢为谏议大夫，召归，道病，卒于建阳驿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1159553_comment'></div>泉人闻之，倾一州来会哭，久不忍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1159553_comment'></div>朝廷举瘤典，赐一子官，所以慰其旅魂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1159553_comment'></div>公仪相魁颀，有伟量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1159553_comment'></div>与人接，坦然必尽其诚，不露形迹，亦不设机键。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1159553_comment'></div>尤笃于孝友，常恨禄不逮亲，居多感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1159553_comment'></div>凡俸赐悉分惠宗党，不问疏密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1159553_comment'></div>姑姊数人孀且老，皆迎归奉之，以终其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1159553_comment'></div>又为外姻之贫者毕嫁娶，复与营其生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1159553_comment'></div>教子舍悉用经术，而济之以严法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1159553_comment'></div>得任子，不与奏，盖欲使其自致也，故诸子多能践其世科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1159553_comment'></div>公没后，布衣者尚三人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1159553_comment'></div>噫，公年十九时已入官，寿虽止五十五，而其间从政者几四十年，可谓久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1159553_comment'></div>事两朝不懈夙夜，国家每有急难处，必首被选委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1159553_comment'></div>又在计庭，更入任不得解，迹其从来，不为不遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1159553_comment'></div>中外望归，谓必大用，天子亦屡欲用之，而公素方整守道，权痈者多不说，故每为其所间而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1159553_comment'></div>公惟所任莫不竭其力，不以抑压自懑而遂浮沉于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1159553_comment'></div>向若得所用如人之所望者，经纶设施，布宣光昭，其为功德，非古贤孰与校之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1159553_comment'></div>娶罗氏，谏议大夫延吉之女，邺王绍威之孙，封宜城县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1159553_comment'></div>六男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1159553_comment'></div>球，湖州德清尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1159553_comment'></div>蠹，将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1159553_comment'></div>琚，司封员外郎、两浙转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1159553_comment'></div>糵，河阳司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1159553_comment'></div>璩，秘书著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1159553_comment'></div>或自科举，或由荫授，方以才名并进而不幸继亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1159553_comment'></div>琦，相仁宗皇帝，被遗制立今天子，为门下侍郎、兼兵部尚书、同中书门下平章事、昭文馆大学士、卫国公，望临天下，瞕冠列辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1159553_comment'></div>以公积德储庆，所宜身享厚报，然恨早世，不克待其发，而发于丞相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1159553_comment'></div>丞相以似以继，其传之者又可涯耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1159553_comment'></div>二女，归于卫尉卿高志宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1159553_comment'></div>丞相贵，累赠公与祖尚书、曾祖永济三代，并太师、中书令兼尚书令，又启魏、燕、冀三国，皆追封为公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1159553_comment'></div>妣罗氏、祖妣李氏、曾妣史氏，亦以魏、燕、齐三国追封为太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1159553_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_114_1159553'>士孰不官，公官独难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1159553_comment'></div>使临东夷，跨海渺漫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1159553_comment'></div>指摩出师，势分敌患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1159553_comment'></div>王始倔强，恃远且艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1159553_comment'></div>视诏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_118_1159553", 1159553, "Clauses/380/Comments/0")'>抹剌</span>，不奉以虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1159553_comment'></div>公怒移书，以诃以谰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1159553_comment'></div>辟以祸福，日星之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1159553_comment'></div>王虽岛酋，闻义惕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1159553_comment'></div>发兵矷粮，革顽易悭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1159553_comment'></div>对卢耨萨，伏命馆门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1159553_comment'></div>能俾远夷，举国奔职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1159553_comment'></div>不惮己劳，不畏邻隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1159553_comment'></div>又俾强虏，敛其毒螫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1159553_comment'></div>二邦由公，一举斯得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1159553_comment'></div>继走朔陲，议收戈蝞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1159553_comment'></div>坐策立判，虏癚不施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1159553_comment'></div>不为其欺，国不挫威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1159553_comment'></div>两使外御，天子再怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1159553_comment'></div>益之众美，大用是宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1159553_comment'></div>而卒不用，谗人之为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1159553_comment'></div>复不永年，道卒遐裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1159553_comment'></div>与考同之，勤官攸致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1159553_comment'></div>位不都躬，萃于幼嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1159553_comment'></div>曰将曰相，瞕德名世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1159553_comment'></div>本支原流，公得何异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1159553_comment'></div>何以畀之，天相其类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1159553_comment'></div>天实使然，人亦靡然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1159553_comment'></div>志诸寞然，其昭昭然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1159553_comment'></div>嘉祐八年十一月十四日建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1159553_comment'></div>武宁章友直篆额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1159553_comment'></div>中书省玉册官王克明萚亿刊<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1159553_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_145_1159553'>州：原无，据《金石萃编》、《彰德府志》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_145_1159553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159553'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_144_1159553_0'>⑴ 嘉庆《安阳县志·金石录》卷五，民国二十二年铅印本。又见《金石萃编》卷一三五，乾隆《彰德府志》卷二七。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1159553_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　本年范纯祐卒，为撰墓志铭。作品：《范纯祐墓志铭》<div id='poem_1159557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>范纯佑墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159557")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159557'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159557'>仆天圣初始识范文正公于海陵，未几公游文馆，仆再举进士来京师，又见之，公益厚我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159557_comment'></div>间或造其门，目公傍一童子方十岁许，神重气远，如老成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159557_comment'></div>仆窃询焉，即公之长子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159557_comment'></div>已能诵《诗》、《礼》，泛读诸书，为文章籍籍有可称者，所与游皆一时之俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159557_comment'></div>时天下庠序未甚兴，公典姑苏，首建郡学，聘安定胡瑗为先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159557_comment'></div>瑗条立学规良密，生徒数百，多不率教，公患之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159557_comment'></div>君尚未冠，辄白于庭，入学，齿诸生之末，尽行其规约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159557_comment'></div>久之，人皆随而不敢犯，自是苏之学遂为诸郡倡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159557_comment'></div>宝元中，西戎叛，一方尽惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159557_comment'></div>公连易关陜官，皆不出兵间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159557_comment'></div>君侍行，日与将卒错处，钩微镘隐，悉得其良驽，由是公任人无失而屡有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159557_comment'></div>公帅环庆也，议城马铺寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159557_comment'></div>寨翨贼境，贼惧城成而扼其冲，故常寇挠之，使我不得城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159557_comment'></div>君率兵驰据其地，贼众大至，且战且督役，数日而成，一路恃以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159557_comment'></div>人又知君材武有足嘉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159557_comment'></div>后公以谗罢知政事，君亦逡巡于仕进间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159557_comment'></div>从公之邓，暴得疾，昏不省事，废卧许昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159557_comment'></div>仆守淮西，过其家省之，犹能感慨道忠义，问仆之来，公耶私耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159557_comment'></div>仆曰：「公」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159557_comment'></div>曰「公则可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159557_comment'></div>噫，人一有疾，已不能自顾其形骸，奚暇他恤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159557_comment'></div>如君病昏，身已弃而尚不忘公忠，岂非根乎至性，第昏于事而性终不昧耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159557_comment'></div>兹尤异于人，可贵重而不可学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159557_comment'></div>病十九年，卒于襄邑弟纯仁之官舍，年四十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159557_comment'></div>君英悟天得，尚节行，事父母尽孝养，未尝去左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159557_comment'></div>文正爱之甚，日夕以讲求道义为乐，亦不欲其远去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159557_comment'></div>君虽文学自富，固不肯应乡里举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159557_comment'></div>不得已，以荫授守将作监主簿，亦暂为岐下司竹监，非其好也，即解去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159557_comment'></div>使君寿且不病，得施其所有于时，良能美业其少诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159557_comment'></div>君名纯佑，字天成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159557_comment'></div>娶长葛李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159557_comment'></div>一男正臣，守太常寺太祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159557_comment'></div>一女，嫁故人子进士元殳，早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159557_comment'></div>纯仁谋归葬河南万安山先垄之侧，行有日，走京师来乞铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159557_comment'></div>仆已铭其父，今又铭其子，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159557_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1159557'>君之才之贤，宜有禄有年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159557_comment'></div>一命而尽不复迁，病十九年不复痊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159557_comment'></div>今其云亡报已骞，英名不隐兮何足叹！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159557_comment'></div>《皇朝文炮》卷一三九。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1159557_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年5月13日</a>　皇太后出手书还政，不干预其撤帘，结果似乎不悦。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年5月16日</a>　讨论积弊应当逐渐整改。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年闰5月13日</a>　与英宗讨论用人之道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年8月</a>　与韩琦有贴，商量恢复武举之事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年冬</a>　因足疾上章乞求补外郡，不许。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　英宗再赐仁宗遗物，力辞不受。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年4月</a>　英宗诏议崇奉濮安懿王典礼事，廷臣争论纷纭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　上奏乞罢枢密使职位。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年夏末</a>　与欧阳修书，修有回书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年7月5日</a>　出为镇海节度使、同平章事、判河阳，封祁国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　王拱辰有书启贺出镇河阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　王安石有上书。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e6fdda1e736a454ea95cb3d4e53dfbb9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e6fdda1e736a454ea95cb3d4e53dfbb9");'><span id='e6fdda1e736a454ea95cb3d4e53dfbb9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>，65岁</div><div id='e6fdda1e736a454ea95cb3d4e53dfbb9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年4月1日</a>　本日觐见神宗，辞集禧观使。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='eb489e78cf5f4b50af7a4fefbe443b04_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eb489e78cf5f4b50af7a4fefbe443b04");'><span id='eb489e78cf5f4b50af7a4fefbe443b04_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>，66岁</div><div id='eb489e78cf5f4b50af7a4fefbe443b04' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年1月</a>　召还京师。有与李师中帖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　上奏，乞给流民以闲田获生养。作品：《论河北流民奏》<div id='poem_1159512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论河北流民奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159512")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159512_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159512'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159512'>臣昨在汝州，窃闻河北流民来许、汝、唐、邓州界逐熟者甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159512_comment'></div>臣以朝廷前许请射系官田土，后却不令请射，尽须发遣归还本贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159512_comment'></div>臣访闻流民必难发遣得回，既已流移至此，又却不得田土，徒令狼狈道路，转见失所，遂专牒本州通判张恂立便往州界诸县流民聚处一一相度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159512_comment'></div>或发遣情愿人归还本贯，或放令前去别州，或相度口数给与民田土，或自令樵渔采捕，或计口支散官粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159512_comment'></div>诸般救济，庶几稍可存活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159512_comment'></div>内只有给田一项，违著朝廷后来指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159512_comment'></div>比欲奏候朝旨，又为流民来者日益多，深恐救恤稍迟，转有死损，遂且用上项条件施行去后，方具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159512_comment'></div>寻准中书劄子，奉圣旨一依奏陈事理，其后来者即教不得给田，候春暖劝谕令归上路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159512_comment'></div>后方知其馀州军所到流民，不拘新旧，并只用元降朝旨，尽不许给与田土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159512_comment'></div>臣其时以急于赴召，不及再有奏陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159512_comment'></div>自襄城县至南薰门共六程，臣见缘路流民，大小车乘及驴马驰载以至担仗等，相继不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159512_comment'></div>臣每逢见逐队老小，一一问当，及令逐旋抄劄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159512_comment'></div>只路上所逢者，约共六百馀户，四千馀口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159512_comment'></div>其逐州县镇以至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1159512", 1159512, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>道店</span>中已安下，臣不见者，并臣于许州驿中住却一日，路上之人臣亦不见者，比臣曾见之数，恐又不下一二百户，三二千口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159512_comment'></div>都计约及八九百户，七八千口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159512_comment'></div>其前后已过，并今未来及有往唐、邓、莱州等处，臣所不见者，又不知其数多少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159512_comment'></div>扶老携幼，累累满道，寒饿之色，所不忍见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159512_comment'></div>亦有病而死者，随即埋于道傍，骨肉相聚，号泣而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159512_comment'></div>臣亲见而问得者，多是镇、赵、邢、洺、磁、相等州下等人户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159512_comment'></div>以十分为率，约四五分并是镇人，其馀五六分即共是赵州与邢、洺、磁、相之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159512_comment'></div>又十中约六七分是第五等人，三四分是第四等人及不济户与无土浮客，即绝无第三等已上之家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159512_comment'></div>臣逐队遍问，因甚如此离乡土，远来他州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159512_comment'></div>其间甚有垂泣告者，曰本不忍抛离坟墓骨肉及破货家产，只为灾伤物贵，存济不得，忧虑饿杀老小，所以须至趁斛斗贱处逃命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159512_comment'></div>又问得有全家起离，来更不归者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159512_comment'></div>亦有减人口暂来逐熟，候彼中无灾伤，斛斗稍贱即却归者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159512_comment'></div>亦有去年先令人来请射或买置田土，稍有准备者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159512_comment'></div>亦有无准备望空来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159512_comment'></div>大约稍有准备来无一二，馀皆茫然，并未有所归，只是路上逐旋问人，斛斗贱处便去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159512_comment'></div>臣窃闻有人闻于朝廷，云流民皆有车仗驴马，盖是上等人户，不是贫民，致朝廷须令发遣却归本贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159512_comment'></div>此说盖是其人只以传闻为词，不曾亲见亲问，但知却有车乘行李次第颇多，便称是上等之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159512_comment'></div>臣每亲见有七八量大车者，约及四五十家，二百馀口；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159512_comment'></div>四五量大车者，约及三四十家，一百馀口；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159512_comment'></div>一两量大车者，约及五七家，七十口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159512_comment'></div>其小车子及驴马担仗之类，大抵皆似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159512_comment'></div>大车并是彼中乡村相近邻里，或出车乘，或出驴牛，或出绳索，或出搭盖之物，递相并合，合作一队起来，所以行李次第力及大户也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159512_comment'></div>今既是贫下之家，决意离去乡土，逃命逐熟，而朝廷须令发遣却回，必恐有伤和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159512_comment'></div>臣亦曾子细说谕，云朝廷恐你抛离乡井，欲拟发遣却归河北，不知如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159512_comment'></div>其丈夫妇人皆向前对曰：「便是死在此处，必更难归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159512_comment'></div>兼一路盘缠已有次第，如何得归？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159512_comment'></div>除是将来彼中有可看望，方有归者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159512_comment'></div>此已上事并是臣亲见亲问，所得最为详悉，与夫外面所差体究之人不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159512_comment'></div>簿、尉、幕职官畏惧州府，州府畏惧提、转，提、转畏惧朝省，不敢尽理而陈述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159512_comment'></div>或心存谄妄，不肯说尽灾患之事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159512_comment'></div>或不切用心，自作卤莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159512_comment'></div>申陈不实者，万不侔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159512_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，早赐指挥，京西一路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159512_comment'></div>如流民到处，且将系官荒闲田土及见佃人占剩无税地土，差有心力、向公官员四散分俵，各令住佃，更不得逼逐发遣，却归河北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159512_comment'></div>其馀或与人家作客，或自能樵渔采捕，或支官粟计口养饲之类，更令中书检详前后条约，疾速严行指挥约束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159512_comment'></div>所贵趁此日月尚浅，未有大段死损之人，可以救恤得及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1159512_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年2月2日</a>　加门下侍郎、同平章事、昭文馆大学士、监修国史。时以病在告。陈舜俞有贺启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年2月27日</a>　上奏论灾荒事。作品：《论灾变而非时数奏》<div id='poem_1159513' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159513' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159513?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论灾变而非时数奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁二年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年2月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159513")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159513_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159513'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159513'>臣伏见近岁以来，灾异频数，天文变于上，地理震于下，人情恐惧，物论纷纭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159513_comment'></div>臣被诏至都，复用为相，虽蒙给假治疾，未遑朝见而坐于私室，如在冰渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159513_comment'></div>况蒙累遣使臣，促令陛对，惊惶陨越，寝食不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159513_comment'></div>然偶于灾异之间，或闻有说者不近正道，臣甚忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159513_comment'></div>比俟入见日面具开陈，又恐差缓，盖救患不可不急，施惠不可后时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159513_comment'></div>臣夙夜揣摩，事无大于此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159513_comment'></div>今遽以狂瞽，上渎冕旒，切望圣慈，更赐裁择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159513_comment'></div>伏闻陛下自始即位，躬亲万几，每有凶灾，忧形玉色，孜孜询访，以求闻失，此真得修讲朝政，答谢天谴之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159513_comment'></div>然臣窃知累有人奏，请凡百灾变，皆系时数，不由人事者，不知有之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159513_comment'></div>若诚有之，此乃奸人谄佞之说，上惑圣聪，臣所谓不近正道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159513_comment'></div>陛下明睿英哲，必不信纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159513_comment'></div>又虑奸人口才捷给，能以甘辞，致陛下或时信之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159513_comment'></div>信则恤灾救患，答谢天谴之意，有时而怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159513_comment'></div>怠则亏陛下之德，损陛下之政，不为宗社生民之福，无甚于此焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159513_comment'></div>臣上所云天变地震，此天下皆知之，皆见之，大可惧者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159513_comment'></div>昔仲尼作《春秋》，不书祥瑞而独书灾异者，盖欲以警戒人君，使恐惧修德，以应天地之变，不闻以灾异归之于时数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159513_comment'></div>至西汉董仲舒传仲尼《春秋》之学，对武帝策曰：「臣观天人相与之际，甚可畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159513_comment'></div>国家将有失道之败，天乃先出灾害以谴告之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159513_comment'></div>不知自省，又出怪异以警惧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159513_comment'></div>尚不知变，而伤败乃至」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159513_comment'></div>董仲舒为西汉群儒之首，所陈灾异，谓尽由朝政而致，岂虚语哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159513_comment'></div>亦不闻以灾害怪异归之于时数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159513_comment'></div>夫上天之变，幽眇高邈，下民或有不见而不知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159513_comment'></div>若数路地震之异，河北特甚，则人皆见之而亲被其害，不可讳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159513_comment'></div>因而人民流散，舍弃坟墓骨肉而适他土，去如鸟兽，茫茫不知所止，饿冻病疾，死于道路者不少，甚可痛惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159513_comment'></div>孟子对梁惠王曰：「涂有饿莩而不知发，人死，则曰『非我也，岁也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159513_comment'></div>是何异于刺人而杀之，曰『非我也，兵也』？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159513_comment'></div>王无罪岁，斯天下之民至焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159513_comment'></div>孟子独得圣人之道为最深，而劝梁惠王专尚仁政，不可罪岁，是亦足以为后世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159513_comment'></div>陛下宜深信而行之，可以回灾异为嘉祥，变祸患为纯嘏，致宗社生民之福，岂有穷也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159513_comment'></div>其奸人亏德损政，谄佞不正之语，必不可令眩惑于其间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159513_comment'></div>又臣少时读书，颇尝探寻天人之理，窃怪有唐韩愈、柳宗元、刘禹锡三子谈天皆不得其要，臣今试陈其梗概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159513_comment'></div>夫太极既判，遂生两仪，形而上者曰天，形而下者曰地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159513_comment'></div>天地之间，盖载者曰万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159513_comment'></div>万物至众，不出乎动与植而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159513_comment'></div>植物不灵，不能有所运用造作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159513_comment'></div>惟动物为有命，比植物为灵，然亦未能为善恶，知喜怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159513_comment'></div>独夫人，又动而有灵者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159513_comment'></div>可以为善，可以为恶者，是人人自为者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159513_comment'></div>自为善、自为恶者皆小焉，天地亦随而应之以祸以福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159513_comment'></div>故《书》曰「作善降之百祥，作不善降之百殃」，《易》曰「作善之家，必有馀庆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159513_comment'></div>作不善之家，必有馀殃」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159513_comment'></div>盖祥与殃祇及其人与家者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159513_comment'></div>夫所谓可以喜可以怒者，非人人之喜怒也，天下人之喜怒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159513_comment'></div>天下人之喜怒，实系乎帝王之所为而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159513_comment'></div>帝王所为之政和，则天下人喜，人喜则其心亦和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159513_comment'></div>和气既生，充于上下，天地自然以和气应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159513_comment'></div>天地气和，则阴阳顺，百谷成，衣食自丰，夭横不作，故民跻富寿，常怀乐康，虽欲使之为乱而叛去，必不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159513_comment'></div>若帝王之政不和，则天下之人不喜，不喜则悲愁怨怒，心亦不和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159513_comment'></div>不和之气既生，天地自然以不和之气应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159513_comment'></div>天地之气不和，则阴阳不顺，百谷不成，衣食不丰，夭横并作，故民皆穷困离散，父母兄弟妻子不能相保，其不思为乱而叛去者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159513_comment'></div>天下之喜怒，所以能感动天地，致祸于国家如此之可必者何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159513_comment'></div>本缘天地万物，通是一气所生，无有纤间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159513_comment'></div>惟是气之清者为天，气之浊者为地，清浊之馀气，散于天地之间，是为万物，万物之最灵者为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159513_comment'></div>以此观之，天地万物，同为一类，则最灵之人，岂不能以众喜众怒之气感动天地而致福致祸于国家者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159513_comment'></div>是故先圣以万物中，独以人配天地，谓之三才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159513_comment'></div>是知人者，与天地本同而末异，体均而气通，不可轻视虚用之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159513_comment'></div>为帝王者，宜先以仁政调和人心，使之安乐自固而不叛去，以为国家永永之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159513_comment'></div>舍此而望天地顺成，天下无事，决不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159513_comment'></div>《尚书·洪范》九畴，八曰庶徵，谓人君行肃、乂、哲、谋、圣五善道，则雨、旸、燠、寒、风五气时而为其休徵，乃百谷用成，俊民用章，家用平康也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159513_comment'></div>人君行狂、僭、豫、急、蒙五恶道，则雨、旸、燠、寒、风五气常而为其咎徵，乃百谷用不成，俊民用微，家用不宁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159513_comment'></div>夫雨、旸、燠、寒、风，虽先后说之，实则一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159513_comment'></div>然而可以为休，可以为咎者，只系乎人君为善为恶而遂分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159513_comment'></div>《洪范》者，二帝三王所行之常道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159513_comment'></div>后之君人者，当信而师尚之，不可谓陈迹不信用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159513_comment'></div>信之则为福，不信则为祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159513_comment'></div>《书》又曰：「天视自我民视，天听自我民听」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159513_comment'></div>又曰：「天聪明，自我民聪明，天明畏，自我民明威」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159513_comment'></div>夫天本无心无耳目，亦无喜怒爱威，作《书》者假视听聪明以为之说，故《易》曰「圣人以神道设教」者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1159513_comment'></div>其实只缘天地人本是一气，善恶动静必然相应合若符契，间不容发，无谓天人形体隔绝至远，便谓两不相干而不以为信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1159513_comment'></div>气既相贯，气动则应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1159513_comment'></div>人有喜怒，天应如响，亦犹冬至一阳生，夏至一阴生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1159513_comment'></div>其气眇然，人不可得而见，惟以葭灰验之，无不刻期以应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1159513_comment'></div>天下人喜怒之气能感动天地之气，亦皆刻期而应也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1159513_comment'></div>是故治天下者，直宜以仁政悦民心，和民气，使其气自通于天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1159513_comment'></div>日星山泽，又皆有神灵主之，则必能默观君人者所为善恶及人之善恶，助其自然之气，降福降祸，岂不尤速耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1159513_comment'></div>岂不尤可惧耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1159513_comment'></div>以此益见天地灾变不可尽归之于时数，而不修人事以应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1159513_comment'></div>然可以归之时数者，故时亦有焉，独尧水汤旱是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1159513_comment'></div>夫尧、汤之为君，必不使人心有不和之气以感动天地而致其水旱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1159513_comment'></div>盖尧、汤大圣人，其佐亦贤，上下协心戮力，无一夫不获，无一物失所，故其水旱不得已可以归之于时数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1159513_comment'></div>然虽有水旱之灾，而不闻有重役横敛、劳民惊众之事，亦不闻有流移播散、冻馁死亡于道之人，惟闻常有九年之蓄，民无菜色，而天下奉尧、汤亦如无水旱之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1159513_comment'></div>爱之如父母，敬之如神明，人心熙熙，和气不减，乃是虽遭水旱而民不被其害，国不忧其危也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1159513_comment'></div>自秦汉以降则不然，凡有灾变怪异，皆由时君世主不能举直错枉，用贤退不肖，复有不能行善道、施仁政、悦民心、和民气，此其以人事致天地灾异必然之理也，必不可归之于时数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1159513_comment'></div>灾异既作，又不能恐惧修省，行消复之道，坐视苍生赤子弃坟墓，离乡土，父母妻子兄弟奔逃播徙，不能相保守，往往君自君，臣自臣，民自民，不相为恤而不加救拯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1159513_comment'></div>民既如此被其害，而不悲愁怨怒，以思为乱者，鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1159513_comment'></div>民既怨怒思乱而国不危者，又鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1159513_comment'></div>彼既上下乖戾，不能同心协力，以致灾变害民而危亡其国，乃妄欲比尧、汤水旱，以己之所致灾异归于时数，是欺天欺民之甚也，胡可信耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1159513_comment'></div>夫地者，至大至厚至静，不可动摇之物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1159513_comment'></div>古今固亦有震动之时，随其所震大小远近，必灾患以应之，然未尝闻数路皆震也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1159513_comment'></div>震且不一，有日或十数震者也，又不一日而止，有至今踰半年尚震而未止者也，是岂不为大灾害耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1159513_comment'></div>大怪异耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1159513_comment'></div>此陛下正当穷究致震之由，推至诚，行至德，思所以厌塞其变，以谢天之谴告焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1159513_comment'></div>不然，则恐董仲舒所谓「败伤乃至」者，必将不能免也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1159513_comment'></div>陛下即位未久，而天下但闻圣德勤俭恭孝，不闻有过，此变非由陛下而致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1159513_comment'></div>然陛下若不为祖宗任其事，则天地之变，谁复可以任之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1159513_comment'></div>陛下既任其事，则固宜兢兢业业，夙夜忧勤，登用正人，兴行正道，思与天地合其德而济之以不懈，使天下皆知陛下恐惧修省，视民如伤，悦其心，和其气，则天地之气亦和而应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1159513_comment'></div>茍如此，何患灾异之不息，人民之不安乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1159513_comment'></div>其奸人谋身害国，罪在杀无赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1159513_comment'></div>其所说，愿陛下绝之，不复留于心术而稍有所惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1159513_comment'></div>其为宗社之福，邦家之庆，必不出乎此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1159513_comment'></div>若陛下万一惑其所说，以灾异归于时数，而圣怀坦然，不以为惧，有司之不职者不加择，政事之不平者不加治，万民穷困失所者不加恤，天下人心必益愁怨而不喜，则阴阳之气何由而和，天地之变何由而息也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1159513_comment'></div>大凡奸佞之人，阿谀巧诈，善移人主之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1159513_comment'></div>其说虽目前可喜，而终无益于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1159513_comment'></div>其大指已达者不过欲持身固禄，未达者不过欲希进厚己，而都不以生灵祸福、国家安危为念也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1159513_comment'></div>是可谓大忍人也，大奸邪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1159513_comment'></div>夫违天贼民，背公弃理，臣故曰罪在杀者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1159513_comment'></div>此须陛下详观其语，熟察其意，复以其人前后所为而参考之，则邪正自见，必不能逃圣鉴矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1159513_comment'></div>臣蒙陛下召作宰相，以疾尚未能一对天表，而不避忤犯，辄敢恳恳如此之切者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1159513_comment'></div>盖观今灾变不与常等，实恐奸人以脂韦善柔之说，移陛下忧劳之志，安陛下克责之心，而致陛下不专心于救患恤灾，以误陛下至大之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1159513_comment'></div>惟圣慈深赐裁察，非臣之幸，乃天下之幸，宗庙社稷之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1159513_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_111_1159513'>〔贴黄〕臣以此奏词颇繁多，然以诚激于中，惟恐陛下未赐信，察臣所以务尽犬马之志，故不觉词之多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1159513_comment'></div>然直书实事，文字鄙拙，不敢徒事章句而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1159513_comment'></div>伏望陛下万几之馀，时赐一览，必亦粗有裨益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1159513_comment'></div>如陛下未以为狂妄之罪，即臣方敢更以管穴之见，仰尘天听也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_114_1159513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159513'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋名臣奏议》卷四二。又见《宋会要辑稿》瑞异三之三五。第三册第二一二一页《历代名臣奏议》卷三○二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1159513_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年2月</a>　久病不出，以至范纯仁上奏，颇有微辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年3月</a>　上朝觐见入对。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年3月21日</a>　再论灾变。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年4月1日</a>　有奏。作品：《请终丧复乐奏》<div id='poem_1159469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请终丧复乐表<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁二年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年4月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159469")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159469'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159469'>三年之丧，既变除于祥禫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159469_comment'></div>六乐之奏，将底协于人神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159469_comment'></div>傥稽礼节之经，曷建中和之极？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159469_comment'></div>冒尘渊听，罄叙愚衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159469_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下迪罔极之纯心，垂无穷之洪覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159469_comment'></div>涵养庶物，相助三灵之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159469_comment'></div>润饰五常，光大累朝之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159469_comment'></div>是宜振动金石，流被管弦，风化多方，鼓舞群品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159469_comment'></div>俾圣神休德，发见乎耳目之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159469_comment'></div>乾坤太和，通融于志气之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159469_comment'></div>然自攀号轩鼎，久缠龙去之悲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159469_comment'></div>遏密舜箫，旷绝凤仪之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159469_comment'></div>兹实朝廷之政，不胜臣子之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159469_comment'></div>望抑厌孝思，讲求古制，敕后夔而庀职，诏神瞽以考声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159469_comment'></div>凡在有生，罔不同乐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1159469_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年4月2日</a>　复上神宗“奉元宪遒文武仁孝”尊号，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年4月</a>　上奏称赞神宗，乞罢听药及同天节上寿，从。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年4月14日</a>　上奏论雨，神宗亲书答复。作品：《论诞日罢宴雨泽之应奏·一》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年4月</a>　上奏致谢，再论君子小人。作品：《论诞日罢宴雨泽之应奏·二》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年6月8日</a>　论京西弓手非便。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年9月</a>　本月推行青苗法，曾议设置局会计。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　为相，擢用韩维、陈襄。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　上疏论王安石。作品：《论王安石并求退疏》<div id='poem_1159520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论王安石并求退疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159520")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159520'>清时窃禄，难逃素食之讥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159520_comment'></div>白首佐朝，遂起蔽贤之谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159520_comment'></div>幸圣明之洞照，举毫发以无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159520_comment'></div>顾此薄材，尚容具位<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159520_comment'></div>切念臣业非经远，识寡通方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159520_comment'></div>少因章句之科，得偕群俊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159520_comment'></div>长脱簿书之秩，获事三朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159520_comment'></div>仁宗之顾遇匪轻，英庙之丁宁尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159520_comment'></div>旋属大人继照，飞龙在天，思肯搆于先基，忽遐遗于万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159520_comment'></div>涧蘋何美，杂圭璧以荐羞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159520_comment'></div>槽驭已疲，复骅骝之共驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159520_comment'></div>殚力虽劳于负岳，小心更甚于履冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159520_comment'></div>果不克堪，遂贻弹劾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159520_comment'></div>如安石者，学强辩胜，年壮气豪，论议方鄙于古人，措置肯谐于僚党？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159520_comment'></div>至使山林末学，草泽后生，放自得之良心，乐人传之异说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159520_comment'></div>蘋蘋者子，譊譊其书，足以干名，足以取贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159520_comment'></div>拖绅朝序者，非安石之党则指为俗吏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159520_comment'></div>圜冠校学者，异安石之学则笑为迂儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159520_comment'></div>叹古人之不生，恨斯文之将丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159520_comment'></div>臣窃观安石平居之间，则口笔丘、旦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159520_comment'></div>有为之际，则身心管、商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159520_comment'></div>至乃忽故事于祖宗，肆巧讥于中外，喜怒惟我，进退其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159520_comment'></div>待圣主为可欺，视同僚为不物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159520_comment'></div>台谏官以兹切齿，谓社稷付在何人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159520_comment'></div>士大夫罔不动心，以朝廷安用彼相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159520_comment'></div>为臣及此，事主若何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159520_comment'></div>臣非不能秉笔华衮之前，而正其非；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159520_comment'></div>覆身青蒲之上，而排其失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159520_comment'></div>重念陛下方当渊默尧、舜，中和禹、汤，同天德之尚阙，待人臣之有体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159520_comment'></div>徒高唇吻，莫补聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159520_comment'></div>且区区晋都，尚有相先之下佐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159520_comment'></div>况赫赫昭代，岂有不和之大臣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159520_comment'></div>愚念及斯，众言陋此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159520_comment'></div>伏乞陛下特申雄断，大决群疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159520_comment'></div>正安石过举之谬，以幸保家邦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159520_comment'></div>白臣等后言之罪，而俾归田里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159520_comment'></div>如其尚矜微朽，处以便藩，不唯有遂于物情，亦以不妨于贤路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159520_comment'></div>如是则始终事圣，史传不附于奸朋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159520_comment'></div>去就为臣，物议庶归于直道。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1159520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159520'><span class='label'>按：</span>《挥麈馀话》卷一，四部丛刊续编本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1159520_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年10月3日</a>　罢相，判河南。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年10月8日</a>　改判亳州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　本年作吕蒙正神道碑。作品：《吕文穆公蒙正神道碑》<div id='poem_1159552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吕文穆公蒙正神道碑<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159552")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159552'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159552'>东平吕公相我太宗、真宗垂二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159552_comment'></div>咸平六年夏，以疾罢归第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159552_comment'></div>大中祥符四年四月十九日，遂不起，年六十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159552_comment'></div>五年十月二十七日，葬于河南府洛阳县金石乡奉先里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159552_comment'></div>后五十七年，其子居简始议琢碑于墓次，请文于里人富某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159552_comment'></div>某义不得辞，辄用纂其世次德业之实，以告诸神曰：吕氏其先，出于炎帝，姜姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159552_comment'></div>虞夏之际，始封于吕，其后遂以所封为氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159552_comment'></div>周初，太公望以功国于齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159552_comment'></div>穆王时，有吕侯为周司寇，王命作《吕刑》以训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159552_comment'></div>至西汉，其裔孙有居东平者，即吕侯之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159552_comment'></div>本大支茂，历世有人，以文武瞕德显名于当时者，伟然相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159552_comment'></div>唐末，徙籍太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159552_comment'></div>国初，迁居洛，今遂为洛阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159552_comment'></div>公讳蒙正，字圣功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159552_comment'></div>太宗太平兴国三年春，首拔进士第，初命将作监丞、通判瘅州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159552_comment'></div>四年代还，会帝征太原刘氏，朝于行在，道受著作郎、直史馆，旋加右拾遗，服银绯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159552_comment'></div>五年，转左补阙、知制诰，服金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159552_comment'></div>八年，迁都官郎中，召入翰林，充学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159552_comment'></div>是冬，擢为左谏议大夫、参知政事，俄皗给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159552_comment'></div>端拱元年，拜中书侍郎，兼户部尚书，同中书门下平章事，监修国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159552_comment'></div>未几，代赵普为上相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159552_comment'></div>淳化二年，罢为吏部尚书，奉朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159552_comment'></div>四年，复为上相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159552_comment'></div>至道元年，除授左仆射，判河南府，兼西京留守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159552_comment'></div>真宗绍位，就加左仆射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159552_comment'></div>咸平三年，诏归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159552_comment'></div>四年，复为上相，益以昭文馆大学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159552_comment'></div>五年，册拜司空，兼门下侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159552_comment'></div>明年感疾，凡七上章求解政事，改太子太师，仍封莱国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159552_comment'></div>以告成泰山，进封徐国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159552_comment'></div>祠后土，又进封许国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159552_comment'></div>及薨，天子震怛，哭甚悲，不能视朝者三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159552_comment'></div>遣使吊祭，赙赐特厚，赠中书令，谥文穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159552_comment'></div>公以诸子位于朝，累赠太师兼尚书令、秦国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159552_comment'></div>始公少时，考妣以口舌偶相戾，遂以异处，然情义内笃，交誓不复嫁娶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159552_comment'></div>考后连佐边幕，妣居洛中，并留公侍焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159552_comment'></div>公每感睵愤懑，绝迹于龙门山，躬事薪汲，力奉慈养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159552_comment'></div>而且痛自刻责以为业，昼夜漏相接，未始少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159552_comment'></div>尝泣泪满所读书，而且痛，日若无以为生者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159552_comment'></div>如是数年，学益富，文益奇，声动天下，士友益附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159552_comment'></div>太祖开宝末，公侍母氏，赴举东都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159552_comment'></div>时太宗以晋王尹开封，闻公名，召见，复索其所著文，大称之，期以公辅之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159552_comment'></div>是秋府荐，甲于乡书，明年即上第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159552_comment'></div>自此七年，参预国政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159552_comment'></div>总十二年，凡七迁，遂作宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159552_comment'></div>领万务必本于仁义教化，而不专尚条约，钧酌衡量，咸适其宜，中外静明，翕然称治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159552_comment'></div>精于选任，辸庸者不得进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159552_comment'></div>久之，知蔡州、金部员外郎张绅以赃败，或谗于帝曰：「绅亦洛人，家甚富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159552_comment'></div>昔吕某方就学，苦贫，恨绅不能如意资其用，今挟权讽下诬以贿免耳，是岂好货者也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159552_comment'></div>帝骤信，立还绅官，而以他事罢公相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159552_comment'></div>公退就常参位，怡然一不自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159552_comment'></div>踰年，帝得绅赃实，始悟，遽黜绅为绛州副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159552_comment'></div>翊日，复以相命公，慰劳优笃，遂及绅事，而公亦不谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159552_comment'></div>帝既爱其能守法度，而复重其沈毅不挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159552_comment'></div>俄欲遣人使朔方，谕中书选才而可责以事者闻，公退以名上，帝不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159552_comment'></div>他日又问，公以前所选对，帝亦不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159552_comment'></div>他日又问益急，公终不肯易其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159552_comment'></div>帝盛怒，投其奏书于地，曰：「吕蒙正何太执耶，必为我易之」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159552_comment'></div>公徐对曰：「臣非执，盖陛下未谅耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159552_comment'></div>因固称其人可使，馀不及，「臣不欲用媚道妄随人主意以害国事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159552_comment'></div>同府皆惕息不敢动，公插笏俛而拾其书，徐怀之而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159552_comment'></div>帝退谓亲信曰：「是公气量，我不如」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159552_comment'></div>既而卒用公所选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159552_comment'></div>复命，大称旨，帝于是益知能任人而加有不可夺之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159552_comment'></div>上元观灯，一夕帝宴近臣于端拱楼，乐车马之艺，左右顾曰：「五代都邑凋丧，闾巷无几人，今其全盛如此，可喜可喜」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159552_comment'></div>公避席曰：「乘舆所在，士庶皆走集，故盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159552_comment'></div>臣常见都外不数里，饥寒而死者甚众，不必尽然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159552_comment'></div>愿陛下视近以及远，苍生之幸也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159552_comment'></div>帝鶁颜不语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1159552_comment'></div>王禹翱名謇谔，时亦在列，闻其对，为之汗下，而公侃然复位，无惧色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1159552_comment'></div>帝以西、北二敌弗服，忿之，常议讨伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1159552_comment'></div>公切谏：「兵者，伤人匮财，不可屡动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1159552_comment'></div>汉武郡国万里外，可谓快其志矣，然天下已困，终悔之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1159552_comment'></div>唐文皇亲征辽碣，手运土木，卒无功而还，亦悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1159552_comment'></div>是二主者，旷百代无比，而用兵皆不免于悔，为后世非笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1159552_comment'></div>陛下及其未有以悔也，惟早慎之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1159552_comment'></div>直宜以道德恩信横于中而澹乎外，则夷狄自宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1159552_comment'></div>与夫命死官，举凶器，校其所不足，与校于无用之地而又痈胜于万一者，岂不远哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1159552_comment'></div>帝倾听褒纳，自是伐议遂寝，但用应兵而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1159552_comment'></div>本朝故事，宰相子起家为水部员外郎，公长子从简当得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1159552_comment'></div>公以延荫太宠，非所以慎官赏励寒畯也，恳辞不拜，癨受将作监丞，因以为著例，于今不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1159552_comment'></div>在河南，会熙陵役作，公念辅政既久，恩宠特殊，羸然曳鄀，谒灵舆于境上，伏地哭几绝，屡哭屡几绝，行路皆哭，皇皇焉不忍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1159552_comment'></div>不得已，乃出私钱三百万助复土之费而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1159552_comment'></div>其在疾告也，降医走使，不绝于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1159552_comment'></div>公以尽瘁积疾，猝未有瘳，累表乞骸骨，优诏不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1159552_comment'></div>既而姑愿归洛，将行，听肩舆至殿门，俾二子掖而登，坐而访问，日昃方罢，二子咸面推以恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1159552_comment'></div>公晚筑园宅于洛，至则以琴觞雅宴自肆于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1159552_comment'></div>间与樵钓野叟骈席而语，不以轩冕累其欢，旷如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1159552_comment'></div>公浑厚渊博，忠亮宽懿，无烦语，不妄顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1159552_comment'></div>与人无亲疏、无高下阶级，而一归于至正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1159552_comment'></div>其为谏诤、为侍从、为执政，凡嘉猷伟画皆不作己出，而密归之于上，惟上自行之，故人无知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1159552_comment'></div>其有不能秘，须论议别白而后方从者遂传焉，则天下称道耸伏，想望其人，邈如神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1159552_comment'></div>自始仕至再罢相，惟在瘅与河南为外委，馀并处内不出，未尝一日远于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1159552_comment'></div>至于河南之行，尚非太皇雅意，盖强出之，将以遗嗣君以结公心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1159552_comment'></div>故章圣初亟复在位，三入相皆首之，所以专其任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1159552_comment'></div>丁内外艰，皆夺情而起，不容终制，不欲使他人代也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1159552_comment'></div>赐第东都，以安其居，俾无外徙之请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1159552_comment'></div>移疾归乡党积十年，卒不许还政，第诏令休息颐养，而密常使人候其安否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1159552_comment'></div>章圣谒陵寝、祀汾阴，再驾西都，皆幸其第，又亲视其疾，思复用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1159552_comment'></div>非公谋谟设施睶运默化，人虽罕得见其迹，而功自被于四海，致时瘅平，则畴能感夫两朝眷遇绝比，如此其至者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1159552_comment'></div>公策名冠天下士，而位登元宰，官至三公，阶、瞕、爵、邑咸第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1159552_comment'></div>勤畏翼翼，乃心王家，周旋始终，毫发无玷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1159552_comment'></div>以老疾恳请而退，天子慊然，犹欲起其废而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1159552_comment'></div>呜呼，盛矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1159552_comment'></div>可谓圣世令德钜人者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1159552_comment'></div>曾王父讳韬，皇主莫州莫县簿，赠太保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1159552_comment'></div>曾王母太原王氏，封许国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1159552_comment'></div>王父讳梦奇，皇户部侍郎，赠太保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1159552_comment'></div>王母颍川郡君陈氏，封邓国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1159552_comment'></div>父讳龟图，皇起居郎，赠尚书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1159552_comment'></div>母彭城刘氏，封徐国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1159552_comment'></div>公掌诰时，会令君朝京师，公跪而泣于令君、徐国，且告曰：「大人母氏皆老矣，不肖子不忍见兹睽忤不偶，愿复故好，敢以死请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1159552_comment'></div>语讫又伏于前，泣下不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1159552_comment'></div>令君、徐国不得已，怜而从之，然终异堂而处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1159552_comment'></div>公晨暮交走，咸尽色养，人于是始知公之纯孝大行于其家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1159552_comment'></div>初娶宋氏，封广平县君，再娶薛氏，封谯国夫人，皆殁于公之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1159552_comment'></div>男十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1159552_comment'></div>从简，驾部员外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1159552_comment'></div>知简，大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1159552_comment'></div>惟简，库部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1159552_comment'></div>承简，虞部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1159552_comment'></div>行简，比部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1159552_comment'></div>次未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1159552_comment'></div>次易简，奉礼部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1159552_comment'></div>务简，光禄少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1159552_comment'></div>居简，龙图阁直学士、尚书兵部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1159552_comment'></div>师简，司农少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1159552_comment'></div>公退居于里，常召诸子立庭下，诲之曰：「吾观旧史，见唐中叶后至周末，乱离相继不绝，卿相往往不得其死而无归全之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1159552_comment'></div>吾幸生盛时，硕茂尊显，今又奉身至此，知夫免矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1159552_comment'></div>矧若曹皆得为王官，其无为世胄子弟之为者以自蹈不淑，且重污吾而将以累吾家」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1159552_comment'></div>由是诸子夙夜相警励，不忘诏教，持身谨敕，咸称善人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1159552_comment'></div>惟龙图公最为肖公，沉识懿行，动有规法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1159552_comment'></div>力以词业，自登名于英俊之域，入践台阁，出更藩服，蔼著嘉绩，稔于舆论，异日必能蹋公之武于廊庙之上而增大乎门构矣，今自海南移典郑州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1159552_comment'></div>馀九人者，先后公皆卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1159552_comment'></div>孙二十五人，曾孙三十一人，并传公之所诲于其父祖，罔敢不率，人于是又知公之义训大施于其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1159552_comment'></div>孙皆有官，而曾孙亦有出仕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1159552_comment'></div>女六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1159552_comment'></div>长嫁光禄寺丞、直集贤院孙暨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1159552_comment'></div>次嫁刑部侍郎，参知政事赵安仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1159552_comment'></div>次嫁太常博士周渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1159552_comment'></div>次嫁观文殿学士、尚书右丞丁度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1159552_comment'></div>次早夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1159552_comment'></div>次嫁永州推官杨巽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1159552_comment'></div>文集二十卷，行于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1159552_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_144_1159552'>天之生贤，而不世出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1159552_comment'></div>出不逢时，亡位而没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1159552_comment'></div>生而无成，不若勿生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1159552_comment'></div>主辰而成，惟公奠京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1159552_comment'></div>初隐而学，四方闻声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1159552_comment'></div>举以魁众，四方益惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1159552_comment'></div>岁始踰七，遂为相臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1159552_comment'></div>相我二宗，太皇粤真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1159552_comment'></div>三相必首，不令后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1159552_comment'></div>善不有已，造宁密陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1159552_comment'></div>事茍秸郁，众皆逡巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1159552_comment'></div>公勇而前，悉心以论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1159552_comment'></div>帝怒斯震，公颜益温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1159552_comment'></div>居若柔弱，语焉不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1159552_comment'></div>及以议诤，骨鲠必伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1159552_comment'></div>公久不渝，一心劬劬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1159552_comment'></div>帝知忠端，始贰终孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1159552_comment'></div>帝嗟乎公，我有不如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1159552_comment'></div>百职具举，万方以胥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1159552_comment'></div>成我太平，匪公曷图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1159552_comment'></div>公处厥位，天子是依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1159552_comment'></div>谗免疾去，天下以思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1159552_comment'></div>进则以道，勤劳饬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1159552_comment'></div>退必以礼，燕乐适之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1159552_comment'></div>曰子痈痈，曰孙群群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1159552_comment'></div>厥有肖子，又绝其伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1159552_comment'></div>天其意者，斯为报与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1159552_comment'></div>文石于墓，无穷之所告与！</div><div id='poem_sentence_171_1159552_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='47b496005fae411f864444e20c923bbb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("47b496005fae411f864444e20c923bbb");'><span id='47b496005fae411f864444e20c923bbb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>，74岁</div><div id='47b496005fae411f864444e20c923bbb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年11月</a>　赴阙参加南郊祭祀配位。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
孟州（河阳）

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年8月</a>　在河阳。为邵雍诗集作诗。作品：《弼观罢走笔书后卷》<div id='poem_217024' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_217024' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_217024'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_217024'>黎民于变是尧时，便字尧夫德可知。<div id='poem_sentence_0_217024_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_217024'>更览新诗名击壤，生生全道略无遗<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书卷二○《首尾吟》附）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_217024_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_217024'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_217024_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年12月</a>　祖无择寄诗，有和答。作品：《答郑州祖龙图见寄原韵》<div id='poem_217033' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_217033' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/217033?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答郑州祖龙图见寄原韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1066年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_217033'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_217033'>坐拥双旌甫浚郊，总戎曾未属鞬櫜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_217033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_217033'>千金寡妙方移疾，二府交修敢惮劳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_217033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_217033'>处世机牙都不竞，摄生权柄急须操。<div id='poem_sentence_2_217033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_217033'>他时病起君恩报，始信林泉属我曹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_217033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_217033'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_217033_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年1月19日</a>　正月英宗驾崩，神宗即位。改为武宁军节度使，进封郑国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年8月</a>　上奏辨君子小人。作品：《上神宗论采听既多当辨君子小人奏》<div id='poem_1159509' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159509' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159509?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上神宗论采听既多当辨君子小人奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平四年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159509")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159509_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159509'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159509'>臣伏自陛下践祚以来，未对天表，蒙差入内供奉官李从政传宣抚问，密旨丁宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159509_comment'></div>特荷非常之眷，绝出流品，仰戴恩德，天地莫量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159509_comment'></div>方属疾恙所缠，步趋殊梗，不得入奉冕旒，略舒臣节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159509_comment'></div>辄以病中传闻一二事，不避斧钺之诛，附李从政上奏，伏惟圣明，一赐观省，不胜大幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159509_comment'></div>臣窃闻陛下始临御，好博采兼听，务广聪明，此古圣王之所尚而君道之至美也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159509_comment'></div>四方鼓舞歌颂，以谓臣下情伪、时政得失，必不能逃圣览，而太平可立致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159509_comment'></div>然其间事体有万类，人品有百端，自古人君采听之际，至难至慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159509_comment'></div>得其人则必以正道，而忠以告之，所说固有益于时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159509_comment'></div>不得其人则专务窥伺，循情阿旨，变曲直者有之，挟爱憎者有之，以至陷害忠良，援引邪僻，张皇威福，耸动观听，大则规取官职，小则希求货财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159509_comment'></div>事至如此，则人君采听之至德，翻成亏损之大弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159509_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159509_comment'></div>盖自古以来，君子常寡，小人常众，人君采听之际，故得人常少，不得人常多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159509_comment'></div>得人少故好事常不足，不得人多故恶事常有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159509_comment'></div>何谓也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159509_comment'></div>君子力行仁义，尊主庇民，为好事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159509_comment'></div>君子则惟道是从，不计身之进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159509_comment'></div>用则进而行道，不用则退而无闷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159509_comment'></div>小人则不然，惟利是向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159509_comment'></div>若为正道所抑，其身不得进，则蹙蹙不肯休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159509_comment'></div>千歧万路，不顾名节，经营钻刺，得其进而后已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159509_comment'></div>既以进身为急，惟知富贵之可乐，则何道之肯守？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159509_comment'></div>何善之肯为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159509_comment'></div>又况君子常为小人所胜，故从古以来，治世少而乱世多者，此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159509_comment'></div>缘君子则可以致治，小人只以致乱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159509_comment'></div>若是君子小人并立于朝，实所难辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159509_comment'></div>盖小人外则文饰其词，所说理道不减于君子，而其心及其所为迹则如水火之异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159509_comment'></div>《书》曰「知人则哲，惟帝其难之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159509_comment'></div>注云：「帝，谓尧也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159509_comment'></div>夫尧为大圣人，仲尼比之如天，而尚未尽得知人之道，况乎居尧之下者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159509_comment'></div>自三代以降，诸侯失国，天子失天下，子孙散而为皂隶，宗社废而为丘墟者，皆因用小人而致之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159509_comment'></div>由此观之，小人岂当亲而用之，又岂当信而任之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159509_comment'></div>臣以谓帝王都无职事，所以别君子小人，乃帝王之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159509_comment'></div>然千官百职，岂尽烦帝王辨之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159509_comment'></div>但精求任天下之事所谓大臣者，不越十数人，不使一小人参用于其间，则千官百职，委诸大臣分而选之，因而渐及天下，州县之吏，莫不得人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159509_comment'></div>顾虽欲乱，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159509_comment'></div>恭惟陛下天赋睿明，神受英略，守祖宗之基业，行尧舜之道德，博取众人之善，欲尽万物之情，为君之难，无甚于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159509_comment'></div>然愿陛下勿谓所采既广，便望所得必多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159509_comment'></div>其间须防奸诈小人，惑乱圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159509_comment'></div>奸谋似正，诈辞似忠，疑似之间，不可不早辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159509_comment'></div>大抵人君生杀权在乎手，不患人不谄奉而密附之也，只患人不肯尽忠而有失即谏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159509_comment'></div>谄奉则顺情而喜人君，喜则富贵可得也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159509_comment'></div>谏之则逆耳而怒人君，怒则殃祸可致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159509_comment'></div>顺情而取富贵者，小人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159509_comment'></div>逆耳而受殃祸者，君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159509_comment'></div>取富贵者，百则百，千则千；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159509_comment'></div>其不避殃祸而欲致人主于无过之地者，百千人中未有一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159509_comment'></div>此惟在陛下审察之，谨择之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159509_comment'></div>既得其人，则专信之，力行之，无容奸佞破坏，则朝廷自理，万方无事，陛下可高枕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159509_comment'></div>又闻昔贤有「英俊沈下僚」之叹，形于讽咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159509_comment'></div>若英俊果沈滞于下，诚宜急取进之，以服士心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159509_comment'></div>其有内行不守，素履非嘉，绩效无闻，公论不与，所以久而不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159509_comment'></div>如此之辈，必恐使其朋党诉以冤抑，妄陈危苦之状，以动渊衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159509_comment'></div>亦愿陛下深察，究其所从来之迹，直俟见其实而进退之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159509_comment'></div>又闻王者端拱垂衣以治天下，然所以劝奖群动而能役使之，俾自奔走于职业者无他，惟官与赏二柄而已，舍此复有何道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159509_comment'></div>官谓爵位，赏谓金帛，茍德称其官，功协其赏，虽官至高、赏至厚，不为过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159509_comment'></div>先王所以重惜之而不妄与人者，非吝之也，盖恐德不称、功不协，人有不平之论，则无以为劝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159509_comment'></div>近日上殿，臣僚颇蒙面赐绯紫者，臣不知当赐与未当赐，但闻多于往时耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159509_comment'></div>爵位、金帛，固不可非次而与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159509_comment'></div>其馀唯章服华显，人亦贵重，亦可以为劝奖之物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159509_comment'></div>若赐之不以劳，又不以年，其有劳有年而得之者不以为贵而反耻之，为不足劝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159509_comment'></div>陛下凡所赐与，本使人知感而劝，令勤其职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159509_comment'></div>若徒俾侥倖者喜，而有劳有年者耻而不劝，则是弃之也，何劝励之有焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159509_comment'></div>《书》曰「车服以庸」，《传》曰「惟名与器，不可以假人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159509_comment'></div>唐有中书令衣绯、宰相衣绿者，以此知不可不稍贵之惜之，以为劝奖之一端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159509_comment'></div>臣少而康壮，已不及人，今既老且病，志气衰索，固无所取，而妄以狂瞽之说尘浼天听者，实恃陛下虚怀待物，无所不容，乃敢然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159509_comment'></div>惟圣慈特赐详览，恐亦有补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1159509_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年9月16日</a>　诏以尚书左仆射、观文殿大学士、集禧观使赴阙，以足疾辞。作品：《论除罢大臣当密奏》<div id='poem_1159510' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159510' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159510?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论除拜大臣当密奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平四年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159510")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159510_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159510'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159510'>臣在河阳，于七、八月间，东有人自京师来，北有人自河朔来，亦有南自蔡、许，西自陕、洛来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159510_comment'></div>皆云：「公以病求解使相，章奏频切，上将许之，却为上尽疑今之两府大臣，复欲用公入相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159510_comment'></div>公既未能步趋拜起，则必召公作宫观使，且留都下，以备访问时政得失」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159510_comment'></div>臣辄每问来者：「此皆朝廷大机宜、大除拜，理当至密，外人何由得知」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159510_comment'></div>来者则云：「此固不可得而知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159510_comment'></div>臣虽闻此说，然终不之信，以谓陛下必不如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159510_comment'></div>既而传闻韩琦、文彦博、陈升之、郭逵相次皆求罢免，又非备礼，并有必去之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159510_comment'></div>以至侍从及主兵之人，各有去位之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159510_comment'></div>其未求去者，非欲不去，盖为求去者已多，未敢有求尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159510_comment'></div>虽勉彊且住，谁复更肯尽心乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159510_comment'></div>若后有许去者，则必节次更有人求去，上挠宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159510_comment'></div>臣续闻此说，略无虚日，则臣向之不信，亦成疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159510_comment'></div>今又蒙差臣充集禧观使，尽如两月前四方传来之语，都无小异，如何使臣不信哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159510_comment'></div>捧诏之日，汗流惊骇，岂有此等国机大事，预令四方人皆知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159510_comment'></div>四方尚知，则两府大臣安有不知者邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159510_comment'></div>陛下既如此疑贰，则执政者不得不求去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159510_comment'></div>臣晓夕思惟，必虑陛下微失防谨，政事泄漏，使人人不安，各怀疑惧，而尽欲解去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159510_comment'></div>此田文所谓「主少国疑，大臣未附，百姓不信」，正如今日陛下之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159510_comment'></div>然魏王时自然如此，今此则或恐陛下圣虑偶有未周，而致其疑也，致其未附也，致其不信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159510_comment'></div>陛下必欲解其疑，使之附而信，莫若罢臣新命，推诚以待诸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159510_comment'></div>必若其间有难久留者，则当徐图去就，所贵事体两全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159510_comment'></div>况韩琦已下七人，尽是两朝顾命大臣，各有忠义之心，岂宜轻议出处，以招天下云云之论哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159510_comment'></div>臣若贪冒恩宠，便为观使，优游辇下，医药尤便，亦无一郡之责，于臣之幸，天下无比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159510_comment'></div>然却有所大不便者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159510_comment'></div>臣若遂居观职，陛下虽都不遣中使传宣抚问，京师四方之人亦疑日有使至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159510_comment'></div>虽或遣使，只是问疾，而都不问及他事，京师四方之人，亦疑凡百朝政，皆来问臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159510_comment'></div>虽或遣使时复问事，臣都不敢答一语，京师四方之人亦疑凡百朝政，臣皆刺口，议论其短长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159510_comment'></div>陛下试思之此三节，果能使人不疑乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159510_comment'></div>臣知万无不疑之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159510_comment'></div>若皆疑之，则今两府八人者，还有不解体者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159510_comment'></div>臣亦知万无不解体者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159510_comment'></div>汉宋昌云「公事公言之，若言私，王者不受私」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159510_comment'></div>今乃使臣于闲宫观中，静坐窃议朝廷之政，致见任大臣一一解体，是公耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159510_comment'></div>是私耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159510_comment'></div>臣亦知京师四方之人，不论贤不肖，必皆谓之私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159510_comment'></div>臣徇从陛下私窃之恩，而辄便当之，则是臣如何人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159510_comment'></div>不惟取罪今世，至于千古之下，亦不能逃责矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159510_comment'></div>臣获罪责于今古之人，固不足惜，然于陛下为君之道，治国之体，还无所损乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159510_comment'></div>臣亦知所损无大于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159510_comment'></div>伏缘天下治乱安危之际，全系天子任人当与不当，若当则更系信与不信尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159510_comment'></div>齐晏子谓用贤而不信是大不信，岂可目为常事而容易措置乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159510_comment'></div>大凡罚一人，众皆惧而不敢犯则罚之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159510_comment'></div>赏一人，众皆悦而有所劝则赏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159510_comment'></div>寻常赏罚，尚须如此谨重，况用舍大臣，岂宜仓卒乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159510_comment'></div>今陛下欲用臣一人，反使众大臣皆解体而不肯住，则陛下岂宜遂其事而必行之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159510_comment'></div>夫人情亦不难回，但请陛下如臣所乞，速放令臣早还本任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159510_comment'></div>仍更临朝，分明宣谕大臣云：「朕欲一见富弼者无他，只为是先朝旧人，都无固必。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159510_comment'></div>他既坚来辞免，即却令归河阳，天下事岂在一富弼乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159510_comment'></div>吾自有诸贤倚赖，无所忧虑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159510_comment'></div>即众心自安，何必更敢求去乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159510_comment'></div>陛下若决能用臣此说，则前失尚可十救五六；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159510_comment'></div>若终不用臣说，则大臣与侍从兵辇官，往往离心离德，无术可救，无事可回，即陛下更与何人共谋国事哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159510_comment'></div>惟愿圣慈，万万熟虑，幸不一向坚用前意而不移，用误大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159510_comment'></div>臣又闻陛下询访太多，听信太杂，因而小人各有希望之心，无所不说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159510_comment'></div>说者既众，是非溷淆，此说已行，他说又夺，展转相效，无有纪极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159510_comment'></div>陛下所闻之事盈塞于心，万务日生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159510_comment'></div>何暇辨别，则所行必有当否，所用必有差失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159510_comment'></div>政无一定之论，人无自保之心，上下纷纭，包藏祸患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159510_comment'></div>臣前附李从政所奏劄子，正为此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159510_comment'></div>更望圣慈并此文字，时赐一览，非臣之幸，乃宗社生灵之幸也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1159510_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年10月2日</a>　以尚书左仆射、观文殿大学士、集禧观使再判河阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年2月9日</a>　本日判汝州，宣召入京。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
万州（万县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='89485950dd2f4cfdafd3d2faad2ad67a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("89485950dd2f4cfdafd3d2faad2ad67a");'><span id='89485950dd2f4cfdafd3d2faad2ad67a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年</a>，28岁</div><div id='89485950dd2f4cfdafd3d2faad2ad67a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年9月</a>　九月，父富言卒于万州任上，时年六十三。富弼前往奔丧。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
新绛
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0b5d6480af0e4fa29460667dd5f56c0d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0b5d6480af0e4fa29460667dd5f56c0d");'><span id='0b5d6480af0e4fa29460667dd5f56c0d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>，31岁</div><div id='0b5d6480af0e4fa29460667dd5f56c0d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　通判绛州，梅尧臣送别。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='54290ea387614e4c9a0f9b1411fd9899_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("54290ea387614e4c9a0f9b1411fd9899");'><span id='54290ea387614e4c9a0f9b1411fd9899_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1036')">1035-1036年</a>，32-33岁</div><div id='54290ea387614e4c9a0f9b1411fd9899' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年2月</a>　居绛州。撰墓志铭一。已失。作品：《陈见素墓志铭》<div id='poem_1159555' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159555' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159555?labeling=true' target='_blank'>范文正公仲淹墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐四年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159555")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159555_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159555'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159555'>皇祐四年夏五月二十日甲子，资政殿学士、户部侍郎范公以疾薨于徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159555_comment'></div>吏走驿马，以公丧闻，天子感慨，一不御垂拱殿朝，特赠兵部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159555_comment'></div>太常考行，谥文正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159555_comment'></div>录孤赙物，悉用加等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159555_comment'></div>中外士大夫骇然相吊以泣，至于珀壑处逸，无不痛惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159555_comment'></div>其孤护帷帻还洛，卜以是年十一月一日壬申，葬于河南县万安山尹樊里先垄之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159555_comment'></div>孤驰使来求铭，将纳于錽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159555_comment'></div>曰：公之先，始居河南，后徙于长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159555_comment'></div>唐垂拱中，履冰相则天，以文章称，实公之远祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159555_comment'></div>四代祖随，唐末尝为幽州良乡主簿，遭乱奔二浙，家于苏之吴县，自尔遂为吴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159555_comment'></div>时中原多故，王泽不能逮远，于是世食钱氏之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159555_comment'></div>苏州粮料判官梦龄，以才德雄江右，即公之曾王父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159555_comment'></div>判官生赞时，初聪警，尝举神童，位秘书监，集《春秋》洎历朝史为《资谈录》六十卷行于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159555_comment'></div>秘监生墉，博学善属文，累佐诸王幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159555_comment'></div>端拱初，随钱俶纳国，终武宁军节度掌书记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159555_comment'></div>公即掌记之第三子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159555_comment'></div>朝廷以公贵，用太保、太傅、太师追赠三代，又择徐、许、越、吴四大国追封王妣陈氏、妣陈氏、谢氏为太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159555_comment'></div>公讳仲淹，字希文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159555_comment'></div>不幸二岁而孤，吴国太夫人以北归之初，亡亲戚故旧，贫而无依，遂再适朱氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159555_comment'></div>公既长，未欲与朱氏子异姓，惧伤吴国之心，姑姓朱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159555_comment'></div>后从事于亳，吴国命始奏而复焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159555_comment'></div>公少举进士，祥符八年中第，调广德军司理掾，权集庆军节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159555_comment'></div>制置使举蝧泰州西溪盐廪，以劳进大理丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159555_comment'></div>又举知兴化县、建州关隶，以吴国老疾辞，监楚州粮料院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159555_comment'></div>丁忧去官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159555_comment'></div>服除，晏丞相以文学荐公于朝，试可，署秘阁校理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159555_comment'></div>时章献皇太后临政，己巳岁冬至，上欲率百僚为寿，诏下草仪注，蝲绅失色相视，虽切切口语而畏惮，无一敢论者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159555_comment'></div>上又专欲躬孝德以励天下，而未遑馀瘤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159555_comment'></div>公独抗疏曰：「人主北面是首，顾居下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159555_comment'></div>矧为后族强翨之阶，不可以为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159555_comment'></div>或宫中用是为家人礼，权而卒于正，斯亦庶乎其可也」。<div class='inline'
