-----title
保定
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cade09619bab4040af3f4ec89b6422b5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cade09619bab4040af3f4ec89b6422b5");'><span id='cade09619bab4040af3f4ec89b6422b5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1045')">1044-1045年</a>，41-42岁</div><div id='cade09619bab4040af3f4ec89b6422b5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年8月25日</a>　奉诏赶往保州节制兵事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年8月29日</a>　上奏论西夏元昊事。作品：《论元昊所上誓书奏》<div id='poem_1159489' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159489' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159489?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论元昊所上誓书奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年8月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159489")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159489_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159489'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159489'>臣近见元昊所上誓书及表奏，辞礼恭顺，一遵朝廷所约，只是疆埸上微有商量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159489_comment'></div>候杨守素等到阙，乞与婉顺商议，示以必和之意，使之深信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159489_comment'></div>不可为其恭顺，却于元约事外，别有诘难邀勒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159489_comment'></div>所宜多方容纳，令无备我之心，则必尽力与契丹相持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159489_comment'></div>若二寇自相杀伐，两有所损，此朝廷之福，天所假也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159489_comment'></div>茍议绝和约，或大段拖延不成，则元昊必复与契丹合，而为患如故，此必然之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159489_comment'></div>臣料契丹必未肯与朝廷绝好，余靖此去，保无他虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159489_comment'></div>将来若遣谢使，所赍谢物，不可过数，茍多无益，更乞深加详择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1159489_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年1月</a>　为河北宣抚使，负责河北东路、河北西路两路的督查扶绥工作。。作品：《乞速令张子奭使契丹行封册之恩奏》<div id='poem_1159492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞速令张子奭使契丹行封册之恩奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159492")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159492'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159492'>若敌使未至而子奭先去，则天下共知事由我出，不待契丹许而后行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159492_comment'></div>今若候敌使至，别无难意，而后方令子奭遂行，则是自以讲和之功归于契丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159492_comment'></div>直待得契丹许意，方敢遣使封册，中国衰弱，绝无振起之势，可为痛惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159492_comment'></div>万一敌使知我尚未封册，词稍不顺，不可却拒元昊而曲就契丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159492_comment'></div>如此，则是朝廷不敢举动，坐受契丹制伏，而又前后反覆，大为元昊所薄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159492_comment'></div>此事余靖奉使时，契丹已许我封册，今但自恐怯，更思变改，臣实不晓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159492_comment'></div>兼契丹西征大衄，山前、山后，非常困弊，必不敢止我此行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159492_comment'></div>伏惟朝廷，据天下之大，四方全盛，若每事听候契丹指挥，方敢施为，使陛下受此屈辱，臣子何安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159492_comment'></div>臣忝预枢辅之列，实为陛下羞之，亦为陛下忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159492_comment'></div>伏乞断自宸衷，不候敌使到阙，速令子奭行封册之恩，则天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1159492_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年1月</a>　因保州兵乱，平叛后，准备诛杀降卒遭到欧阳修抵制。<br /></div>
-----end

许昌（长社）

-----title
青州（益都）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4a8145f936224400828ec4d5055047a2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4a8145f936224400828ec4d5055047a2");'><span id='4a8145f936224400828ec4d5055047a2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1050')">1047-1050年</a>，44-47岁</div><div id='4a8145f936224400828ec4d5055047a2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　在山东。本年次子绍京生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　在山东。本年尹洙卒，闻讯后有作。作品：《哭尹舍人词》<div id='poem_1159558' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159558' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159558?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哭尹舍人词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159558")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159558_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159558'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159558'>亡友河南尹洙，字师鲁，尝为起居舍人、直龙图阁、知渭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159558_comment'></div>乙酉岁谪官汉东，未几稍迁于均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159558_comment'></div>疾且革，访医南阳，以皏范公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159558_comment'></div>医不效，遂没焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159558_comment'></div>时予官汶上，又东徙乎卢，距其没所远甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159558_comment'></div>睵师鲁之不得见，复不得抚其榇一祭其神，因追思其平生所可列，恨未有以卒其志，为辞而哭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159558_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1159558'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159558_comment'></div>人皆贵，君实悴焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159558_comment'></div>人皆富，君实窭焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159558_comment'></div>人皆老，君实夭焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159558_comment'></div>吾知君为深，是三者举非君之志，则吾焉哭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159558_comment'></div>哭必义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159558_comment'></div>始君作文，世重淫丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159558_comment'></div>诸家舛殊，大道破碎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159558_comment'></div>漫漶费词，不立根柢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159558_comment'></div>号类啸朋，争相教惎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159558_comment'></div>上翔公卿，下典书制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159558_comment'></div>君于厥时，了不为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159558_comment'></div>独倡古道，以救其敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159558_comment'></div>时俊化之，识文之诣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159558_comment'></div>今则亡矣，使斯文不能救其源而极其致，吾是以哭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159558_comment'></div>始君为学，遭世乖离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159558_comment'></div>掠取章句，属为文词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159558_comment'></div>经有仁义，曾非所治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159558_comment'></div>史有褒贬，亦弗以思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159558_comment'></div>君顾而睵，嫉时之为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159558_comment'></div>钩抉六籍，睶心以稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159558_comment'></div>上下百世，指掌而窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159558_comment'></div>功不茍进，习无匪彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159558_comment'></div>今则亡矣，使所学不能信于人而用于时，吾是以哭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159558_comment'></div>惟文与学，二事既隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159558_comment'></div>充用而衷，丰于时穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159558_comment'></div>纯深蕴积，资而为德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159558_comment'></div>行乎己而己必裕，行乎家而家必克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159558_comment'></div>今则亡矣，使贤者之行不能移人心而化大国，吾是以哭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159558_comment'></div>积德既成，道随而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159558_comment'></div>谋罔不究，动必有经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159558_comment'></div>列于庭则以蹇谔见黜，用于边则以威怀取宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159558_comment'></div>才望既出，谗嫉以兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159558_comment'></div>酷罚嗣降，愠色不形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159558_comment'></div>今则亡矣，使君子之道不能被天下而致太平，吾是以哭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159558_comment'></div>呜呼师鲁，君生于时，实惟恢奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159558_comment'></div>钟此具美，谓必有光大以奋，康济是期，胡既厚其禀而反速其萎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159558_comment'></div>凡粤中蕴，百无一施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159558_comment'></div>岂茫茫下土，天亦有所不知耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159558_comment'></div>将冥冥上穹，人固非其所司耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159558_comment'></div>何恶不必衅而善不必禔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159558_comment'></div>忠良而夭，险狠而耆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159558_comment'></div>汩淆参错，颠倒乖暌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159558_comment'></div>天其或者世不欲常泰，人不欲常熙？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159558_comment'></div>吾疑夫激者之论，差不得而信之，第于师鲁，哭无已而。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159558_comment'></div>一哭而恸，再哭而咽，三哭而魂离，四哭而肠绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159558_comment'></div>苏而复哭，哭又不足，聊以写吾之哭声而寓于辞，庶不泯没于陵谷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1159558_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年3月18日</a>　因平齐州兵叛有功，除礼部侍郎，不受。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　因黄河泛滥，河北流民奔走青州，有告示安居流民。作品：《擘画屋舍安泊流民事指挥》《救荒活民书》《支散流民斛斗画一指挥》<div id='poem_1159530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159530?labeling=true' target='_blank'>擘画屋舍安泊流民事指挥<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年6月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159530")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159530_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159530'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159530'>当司访闻青、淄、登、潍、莱五州地方，甚有河北灾伤流移人民逐熟过来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159530_comment'></div>其乡村县镇人户，不那趱房屋安泊，多是暴露，并无居止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159530_comment'></div>日下渐向冬寒，窃虑老少人口，别致饥冻死损，甚损和气，须议别行擘画下项：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1159530'>一、州县坊郭等人户，虽有房屋人，缘见是出赁与人户居住，难得空闲屋室，今逐等合那趱房屋间数如后：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1159530'>第一等五间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159530_comment'></div>第二等三间/第三等两间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159530_comment'></div>第四等、五等一间/一、乡村人户，甚有空闲房屋，易得小可屋，今逐等合那趱间数如后：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1159530'>第一等七间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159530_comment'></div>第二等五间/第三等三间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159530_comment'></div>第四等、五等两间/右各请体认。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159530_comment'></div>见今流民不少，在州，即请本州出榜，在县镇乡村，即指挥县司，晓示人户，依前项房屋间数，各令即趱立定日限，须官数足数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159530_comment'></div>内城郭勒厢界管当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159530_comment'></div>其乡村即指挥逐地分耆壮抄点逐等姓名、趱那到房屋间数申官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159530_comment'></div>仍叮咛约束管当人等，不得因缘骚扰，乞觅人户钱物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159530_comment'></div>如有违犯，严行断决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159530_comment'></div>仍指挥州县城镇门头人，常切辨认，才候见有上件灾伤流民老小到门内，其在州则引于司理处出头，其在乡即引于知县处出头，其在镇内即引于监务处出头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159530_comment'></div>各仰逐官相度人数，指定那趱房屋主人姓名，令干当人尽将引押于抄点下房屋内安泊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159530_comment'></div>如门头不肯引领者，许流民于随处官员处出头，速取劝决讫，当使指挥安泊了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159530_comment'></div>如有流民欲前去，未肯安泊者，亦听从便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159530_comment'></div>如有流民不奔州县，直往乡村内安泊者，仰耆壮尽将引领于趱那下房内安泊讫，申报本县及当职官员，躬亲劝诱，逐家量口数各与桑土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159530_comment'></div>或贷种救济，种植度日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159530_comment'></div>内有见在房数少者，亦令收拾小可材料，权与盖造应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159530_comment'></div>若有下等人户，委的贫虚，准无房屋那应，不得一例施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159530_comment'></div>除此擘画之外，如更有安泊不尽老少，即指挥逐处僧尼等寺、道士女冠宫观，门楼廊庑，及更别趱那新居房屋，安泊河北逐熟老小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159530_comment'></div>如有指挥不及事件，亦请当职官员，相度利害，一面指挥施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159530_comment'></div>务要流民安居，不至暴露失所。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1159530_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1159532' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159532' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159532?labeling=true' target='_blank'>支散流民斛㪷画一指挥<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159532")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159532_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159532'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159532'>当司昨为河北遭水，失业流民拥并过河南，于京东青、淄、潍、登、莱五州丰熟处，逐处散在城郭乡村不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159532_comment'></div>当司虽已诸般擘画，采取事件，指挥逐州官吏，多方安泊，存恤救济施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159532_comment'></div>本使体量，尚恐流民失所，寻出给告谕文字，送逐州给散诸县，令逐耆长，将告谕指挥乡村等第人户并客户，依所定石斗出办米豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159532_comment'></div>数内近州县镇，只于城郭内送纳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159532_comment'></div>其去州县镇城远处，只于逐耆令耆长置历受纳，于逐耆第一等人户处，圆那房屋盛贮，收附封锁施行去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159532_comment'></div>日后据逐州申报已告谕到斛㪷数目，受纳各有次第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159532_comment'></div>今体量得饥饿死损，须至令上项五州，一例于正月一日，委官分头支散上件勘谕到斛㪷，救济饥民者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1159532'>一、请本州才候牒到，立便酌量逐县耆分多少差官，每一官令专管十耆或五七耆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159532_comment'></div>据耆分合用官员数，除逐县正官外，请于见任并前资寄居及文学、助教、长史等官员内，须是拣择有行止、清廉干当、素不作过犯官员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159532_comment'></div>仍勘会所差官员本贯，将县分交互差委支散，免致所居县分，亲故颜情，不肯尽公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159532_comment'></div>及将封去帖牒，书填定官员职位、姓名、所管耆分去处，给与逐官收执，火急发遣往差定县分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159532_comment'></div>计会县司，尽时将在县收到赃罚钱或头子钱，并检取远年不用放纸卖钱，收买小纸，依封去式样、字号空数，雕遍印板。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159532_comment'></div>酌量流民多少，宽剩出给印押历子头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159532_comment'></div>各于历子后，粘连空纸三两张，便令差定官员，令本县约度逐耆流民家数，分擘画历子与所差官员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159532_comment'></div>使令亲自收执，分头下乡，勒耆壮引领，排门点检抄诸流民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159532_comment'></div>每见流民，逐家尽底唤出本家骨肉，亲自当面审问的实人口，填定姓名口数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159532_comment'></div>逐家便各给历子一道收执，照證准备请领米豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159532_comment'></div>即不曾差委公人耆壮，抄诸别到作弊，虚伪重砯，请却历子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1159532'>一、指挥差委官抄诸给历子时，子细点检逐处流民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159532_comment'></div>如内有虽是流民，见今已与人家作客，锄田养种，及有钱本机织贩舂诸般买卖，图运过日，不致失所人，更不得一例抄诸姓名，给与历子，请领米豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1159532'>一、应系流民，虽有房舍权时居住，只是旋打州柴草，日逐旋求口食人等，并尽底抄诸，给与历子，令请领米豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1159532'>一、应有流民，老小羸瘦，全然单寒，及孤独之人，只是寻村乞丐安泊，居止不定等人，委所差官员擘画，归著耆分，或在庙寺院安泊，亦使出给历子，请领米豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159532_comment'></div>又不得谓难为拘管，辄敢违弃，却致抛掷死损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159532_comment'></div>请提举官常切觉察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1159532'>一、应系土居，贫穷年老，残患孤独，见求乞贫子筹，仰抄诸流民官员，躬亲检点。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159532_comment'></div>如果不是虚伪，亦各给历子，令依此请领米豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1159532'>一、指挥差委官员，须是于十二月二十五日已前，抄诸集定流民家口数，给散历子了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159532_comment'></div>须管自皇祐元年正月一日起首，一齐支给，不得拖延有误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159532_comment'></div>至日支散，亦不得日数前后不齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1159532'>一、流民所支米豆，十五岁以上，每人日支一升；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159532_comment'></div>十五岁以下，每日给五合；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159532_comment'></div>五岁以下男女不在支给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159532_comment'></div>仍历子头上分别细算定一家口数，合请米豆都数，逐旋依都数支给，所贵更不临时旋讨者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1159532'>一、缘已就门抄诸见流民逐家口数及岁数，则支散日更不令全家到来，只每家一名，亲执历子请领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1159532'>一、逐官如管十耆，即每日支两耆，逐耆并支五日口食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159532_comment'></div>候五日支遍十耆，即却从头支散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159532_comment'></div>所贵逐耆每日有官员躬亲支散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159532_comment'></div>如管五七耆者，即将耆分大者，每日支散一耆，其耆分小者，每日支散两耆，亦须每日一次支遍，逐次并支五日口食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159532_comment'></div>仍预先于村庄明出晓示，及令本耆壮丁四散告报流民，指定支散日分去处，分明开说甚字号耆分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159532_comment'></div>仍仰差去官员，须是及早亲自先到关支斛斗去处，等候流民到来，逐旋支散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159532_comment'></div>才候支绝一耆，速往下次合耆分，不得自作违慢，拖延过时，别至流民归家迟晚，道涂冻露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1159532'>一、指挥差委官员，相度逐处受纳下米豆，如内有在耆分遥远第一等户人家收附，恐流民所去请领遥远，即勒耆壮量事圆那车乘，般赴本耆地分中心稳便人家房屋内收附，就彼便行支散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159532_comment'></div>贵要一耆之内，流民尽得就近请领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1159532'>一、指挥所差官员，除抄诸籍定给散流民外，如有逐旋新到流民，并须官员亲到审问，子细检点本家的实口数，安泊去处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159532_comment'></div>如委不是重砯虚伪，立便给与历子，据所到日分起请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159532_comment'></div>如有已得历子流民起移，仰居停主人，画时令流民将元给历子，于监散官员处毁抹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159532_comment'></div>若是不来申报，及称带却历子，并仰量行科决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159532_comment'></div>不得卤莽重砯给印历子，亦不得阻滞流民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1159532'>一、逐耆各均匀纳下斛米，窃恐流民于逐耆分安泊不均，仰县司勘会，据流民多处耆分，酌量人数，发遣趱并于少处耆分安泊，令逐耆均匀支散救济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159532_comment'></div>若是流民安泊处稳便，不愿起移，即趱并别耆斛斗就便支绛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159532_comment'></div>不得抑勒流民，须令起移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1159532'>一、州县镇城郭内流民，只差委本处见任官员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159532_comment'></div>亦先且躬亲排门抄诸逐户家口数，依此给与历子，每一度并支五日米豆，候食尽挨排日分，接续支给米豆，一般施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_1159532'>一、逐州除逐处监散官员，仍请与通判或选差清干职官一员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159532_comment'></div>往本州界内，往来都大提举诸县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159532_comment'></div>支散米豆官吏，仍点检逐耆元纳并逐官支散文历，一依逐件钤束指挥施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159532_comment'></div>仍亲到支散米豆处，子细体问流民，所请米豆，委得均济，别无漏落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159532_comment'></div>如有官员弛慢，不切用心，信纵手下公人作弊，减鮨流民合请米豆，不得均济，即密具事由，申报本州，别选差官员冲替讫，申当司，不得盖庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1159532'>一、所支斛斗，如州县内支绝已纳到告谕斛斗外，有未催到数目，便且于省仓斛斗内权时借支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159532_comment'></div>据见欠斛斗，立便催纳，依数拨填。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159532_comment'></div>其乡村所纳斛斗，如未足处，亦逐旋请紧切催促，不得阙绝支散，闪误流民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_1159532'>一、每官一员，在县摘差手分、㪷子各一名，随行干官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159532_comment'></div>仍给升、斗各一双，差本县公人三两人当直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159532_comment'></div>如在县公人数少，即权差壮丁<span class='inlineComment2'>（亦不得过三人。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_1159532'>一、所差官员，除见任官外，应系权差请官，如手下干当人并耆壮等，及流民内作过者，本官不得一面区分，具事由押送本县，勘断施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1159532'>一、权差官每月于前项赃罚头子等钱内，支给食直钱五贯文，见任官不得一例支给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_1159532'>一、权差官已有当司封去帖牒，若差见任官员，即请本州出给文字干当，其赏罚一依当司封去权差官帖牒内事理施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_1159532'>一、才候起支，当司必然别州差官，鮂诣逐州逐县耆点检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159532_comment'></div>如有一事一件违慢，本州承牒手分并县司官吏，必然勘罪严断，的不虚行指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_1159532'>一、逐州县镇，候差定官员，将印行指挥画一抄诸一本，付逐官收执，照会施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_70_1159532'>一、勘会二麦将熟，诸处流民尽欲归乡，寻指挥逐州并监散官员，将见今籍定流民，据每人合请米豆数目，自五月初一日算至五月终，一并支与流民充路粮，令各任便归乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_1159532'>一、指挥出榜青、淄等州河口晓示，与免流民税渡钱，仍不得邀难住滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_1159532'>一、指挥青、淄等州，晓示道店，不得要流民房宿钱事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1159532_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_1159532'>右具如前事，须各牒青、淄、潍、莱、登五州，候到，各请遵依前项逐件指挥施行，就报所有当司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1159532_comment'></div>封去帖牒，如有剩数，却请封送当司，不得有违。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1159532_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　本年还有其他奏章，以安顿灾民等事。作品：《乞拨河北逃田为屯田奏》<div id='poem_1159496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞拨河北逃田为屯田奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159496")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159496'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159496'>臣窃闻河朔军储，每岁不减六七百万斛，自来本路赋入外，须更令客旅入中，方得充足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159496_comment'></div>今水灾之后，农民大半流徙，从来沃壤，尽为闲田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159496_comment'></div>又河朔所占地土至多，无由耕稼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159496_comment'></div>臣窃计见入之赋，不过三分之一，别路支拨增添，亦不过十万斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159496_comment'></div>谷价踊贵，必无入中之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159496_comment'></div>则是河北每岁军储，顿亏一半已上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159496_comment'></div>虽朝廷极力救济，臣知无以出办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159496_comment'></div>况别路所拨之物，已是那辍应副，若更减辍两科，则彼自虚竭，必是难为支拨，民力不得不困，国用不得不窘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159496_comment'></div>臣兼体量得河朔流民东走登、莱、潍、密，南奔淮、楚、荆、襄，西至并、代、关、陕，北投幽燕及山后诸镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159496_comment'></div>暌离四散，无所不之，二三年间，唯上等有力，或可归业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159496_comment'></div>自馀流浪忘反，卒无还期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159496_comment'></div>河朔逃田，尽成废弃，河朔军需，无以供亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159496_comment'></div>若不早为擘画，恐朝廷财用殚耗，遂至不支，甚非为国之计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159496_comment'></div>臣尝览载籍，历代备边守戍，多用屯田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159496_comment'></div>赵充国守先零，曹凤守西城，诸葛亮守魏，羊祜守吴，当时皆为戍边颇多，军食不足，尽取营田之利，遂立破敌之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159496_comment'></div>况今陕西、河北缘边，甚有置屯田之处，法制多在，增修不难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159496_comment'></div>臣欲乞朝廷指挥河北州县，去年逃田，随所在拨为屯田，诸处抽差厢军给使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159496_comment'></div>如不足，即募流民，日得数千人，不必比招军人例特支破衣粮，但量给口食，粗令饱足，既免冻馁，必乐服田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159496_comment'></div>况本是农家，不劳教劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159496_comment'></div>或更许收成后十分中少给与一二分，以充赡养之资，则应募者其孰能御之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159496_comment'></div>兼自来经水田土，十倍肥浓，耕凿之功，不甚劳力，但能布种在地，便有厚获之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159496_comment'></div>至于农具牛畜，亦易为经度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159496_comment'></div>或虑灾伤之后，难得牛畜，只用人亦可应急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159496_comment'></div>若朝廷严切指挥，速令兴作，必然今秋便有所入，一二年后，不可胜食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159496_comment'></div>才候流民复业，逐旋据其元地给与，则向时流徙，不患其不归也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159496_comment'></div>方今至急之务，无出于此，伏惟圣慈，早赐裁择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159496_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1159496'>〔贴黄〕臣职在京东，不合频起请河北事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159496_comment'></div>只缘河北流民多在京东，蚁聚蚕食，不无搔扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159496_comment'></div>若河北招诱得流民渐次归业，则京东自然无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159496_comment'></div>又京东见支拨税赋、辇运斛斗救济河北民，甚不易，若河北逃田不废，则人自足食，京东之民，亦得息肩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159496_comment'></div>有此事理相干，臣是以不避越职之过，骤有陈列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159496_comment'></div>伏惟圣慈，特赐矜照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159496_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1159496'>〔贴黄〕此事不必立望十分济事，但略有所得，已胜却尽为闲田，年岁间必大有收入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159496_comment'></div>如相度稍便，须是早降指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1159496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　题石云门山，处青州府城南。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年2月8日</a>　以安抚流民有功，再除吏部侍郎，不受。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年7月11日</a>　加资政殿学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　本年应韩琦之请，作阅古堂诗。作品：《定州阅古堂》<div id='poem_217040' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_217040' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/217040?labeling=true' target='_blank'>定州阅古堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_217040")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_217040_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_217040'>天下十八道，惟河北最重。河北三十六州军，就其中又析大名府定州真定府高阳关为四路，惟定州最要。定为一路治所，实天下要重之最。知是州者，兼本路兵马都部署，居则治民，出则治兵，非夫文武才全，望倾于时者，不能安疆埸屏王室也。然自国初已来，专以武臣帅诸路。庆历七年，甘陵妖贼据城叛，河北妖党相摇以谋应，卒骄将愞，人心大震。天子悟，始议选儒臣帅四路，以督诸将。乃起知郓州资政殿学士给事中昌黎韩公帅真定，以遏乱萌。明年春，贼诛人安。既而夏大雨，河决商胡，东北入于海。河北灾，人复不宁，流徙失业者四出，咸不翅千里，僵殍满道。天子恤然，且虞他癚，遂以公帅定。定既要重天下，宿兵素多，属伤残之后，官民枵困，征赋逃无几而兵不少减。兵袭旧幸歉，益骄以悍。公夙夜裁整，以威以怀，兵之骄不从令者，脁其首恶，斩以徇，略为条教。馀怗怗就约，不敢玟于室。至有调发者，远而弥戢，如公亲临。已而招集逋亡，四流争还，如啼孩奔父母，惟恐其后。至则充然各得其欲，农无废陇，赋有馀粒，不旁诛横敛而上下足。堙漏补罅，一面完固。公既击瞗梗之兵，又育彫瘵之民，左行斧钺，右哺饮食，乱者毕治，亡者毕存。礼法政教，向之人所不得闻者，今渐濡酣饫，无不贯彻。自是边人革其耳目，新其肝肠，优为而乐从，故人易治而功成速也。又明年秋，天子图公之功，诏加大学士。公先尝表其志，幸终三年，不愿亟易也。至天子抑骑召而使即以授，姑遂公请，亦以慰斯人爱公之心也。公惕宠处官，虽无事未尝辄自豫，念兵与民之急，宜无过者。矧临要重之路，忧虞所系，凡是绘画，不可以无法。乃择取历代贤守良将总若干人行事，创大屋，以类相次，绘于周壁，谇之曰阅古堂。盖欲阅古之人所为而为之法也。噫！公雅文盓武，自当视乎古人。且天下方迟公入辅，以致太平，若其安疆埸屏王室，岂庸考古而后能哉？实公冲然，不自有其有，而归乎古人也。其悬知来者，不师绘事而公是师也。虽然，蹋古蒐善，惠人警己，公之意谓其至矣乎！公邮问索诗，因粗序所致之旨，以志其始而示于后。诗曰：</div><div id='poem_preface_217040_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_217040'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_217040'>朔方之兵，劲于九土。<div id='poem_sentence_0_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_217040'>尤劲而要，粤惟定武。<div id='poem_sentence_1_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_217040'>兵劲在驭，用则罴虎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_217040'>失驭而劲，骄不可举。<div id='poem_sentence_3_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_217040'>曰保曰贝，闭壁连阻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_217040'>武爵新<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>守，束手就虏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_217040'>皇帝曰噫，汝武曷取。<div id='poem_sentence_6_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_217040'>有敝必革，以儒于抚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_217040'>公来帅定，始以威怒。<div id='poem_sentence_8_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_217040'>有兵悍横，一用于斧。<div id='poem_sentence_9_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_217040'>连营怛之，胆栗腰伛。<div id='poem_sentence_10_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_217040'>既惧而教，如餔如乳。<div id='poem_sentence_11_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_217040'>以刺以射，以钲以鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_12_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_217040'>无一不若，师师旅旅。<div id='poem_sentence_13_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_217040'>列城自刺，靡不和附。<div id='poem_sentence_14_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_217040'>阴沴为梗，降此大雨。<div id='poem_sentence_15_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_217040'>大河破泄，在河之浒。<div id='poem_sentence_16_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_217040'>民被黜垫，田入莽污。<div id='poem_sentence_17_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_217040'>流离荡析，不得其所。<div id='poem_sentence_18_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_217040'>公戚曰吁，予敢宁处。<div id='poem_sentence_19_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_217040'>乃大招来，乃大保聚。<div id='poem_sentence_20_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_217040'>乃营帛粟，寒衣饥茹。<div id='poem_sentence_21_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_217040'>民归而安，水下孰御。<div id='poem_sentence_22_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_217040'>强弱死生，由公复虑。<div id='poem_sentence_23_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_217040'>曰义曰仁，震<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>肃春煦。<div id='poem_sentence_24_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_217040'>合和蒸天，天顺以序。<div id='poem_sentence_25_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_217040'>公境独稔，爰麦爰黍。<div id='poem_sentence_26_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_217040'>公俗独乐，夫耕妇杼。<div id='poem_sentence_27_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_217040'>人虽曰康，公亦奚豫。<div id='poem_sentence_28_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_217040'>谓此一方，民与兵具。<div id='poem_sentence_29_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_217040'>务剧任重，稽古其裕。<div id='poem_sentence_30_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_217040'>人皆谓公，与古为伍。<div id='poem_sentence_31_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_217040'>公文化民，公武御侮。<div id='poem_sentence_32_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_217040'>何思古人，公不自许。<div id='poem_sentence_33_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_217040'>遂择奇匠，绘于堂宇。<div id='poem_sentence_34_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_217040'>列其行事，指掌可数。<div id='poem_sentence_35_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_217040'>前有古人，在我门户。<div id='poem_sentence_36_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_217040'>后有来者，依我墙堵。<div id='poem_sentence_37_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_217040'>斯堂勿坏，有堂有故。<div id='poem_sentence_38_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_217040'>堂之不存，来者曷睹。<div id='poem_sentence_39_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_217040'>宏乎焕乎，千载是矩。<div id='poem_sentence_40_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_217040'></div><div id='poem_sentence_41_217040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_217040'><span class='label'>按：</span>《皇朝文炮》卷一二。又见《古今图书集成》职方典卷一○五，嘉靖《真定府志》卷一八，道光《直隶定州志》卷二一，民国《定县志》卷一九。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_217040_0'>⑴ 《永乐大典》卷七二四一、《四朝诗》作斯</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_24_217040_0'>⑵ 《永乐大典》作霜</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_217040_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　还在青州任上，再次上救济流民札子。作品：《宣问救济流民事札子》<div id='poem_1159498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣问救济流民事劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24790, "北宋", "富弼", "poem_title_1159498")'>富弼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159498'>臣伏奉圣旨，取索擘画救济流民等事件，今节略编修作四策，具状缴奏去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159498_comment'></div>臣部下九州军，其间近河五州颇熟，逐醵于民，得粟十五万斛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，只令人户就本村耆随处收纳，贵不劳我士民<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159498_comment'></div>又先时已于州县城镇乡村，抄下舍宇十馀万间，流民来者，随其意散处民舍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159498_comment'></div>逐家给一历，历各有号，使不相侵欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159498_comment'></div>仍于历前计定逐家口数及合给物数，令官员诣逐乡逐耆，就流人所居近处，每人日给生豆米各半升，流民至者安居而日享食物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159498_comment'></div>又以其散在村野，薪水之利，甚不难致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159498_comment'></div>似此直养活至去年五月终麦熟，仍各给与一去路粮而遣归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159498_comment'></div>而按籍总三十馀万人，此是于必死之中救得活者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159498_comment'></div>与夫只于城中煮粥，使四远饥羸老弱，每日奔走屯聚城下，终日等候，或得或不得，闪误死者，大不侔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159498_comment'></div>其馀未至羸病老弱，稍营运自给者，不预此籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159498_comment'></div>然亦遍晓示五州人民，应是山林河泊，有利可取者，其地主不得占却，一任流民采掇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159498_comment'></div>如此救活者甚多，即不见数目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159498_comment'></div>山林河泊，地主宁无所损，然损者无大害，而流民活利者便活性命，其利害较然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159498_comment'></div>又减利物，广招兵徒一万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159498_comment'></div>寻常利物，每一人可招三人，或有四五口，及四五万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159498_comment'></div>大约通计不下四五十万人，传云生全百万者，妄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159498_comment'></div>谨具劄子奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1159498_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159498'><span class='label'>按：</span>《救荒活民书》卷三，墨海金壶本。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_1159498_0'>⑴ 第一等两石，第五等三斗而已，民甚乐输。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_1159498_0'>⑵ 多差官员领之，见任不足，即指请前资、寄任、待阙闲官。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1159498_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　本年荐举赵滋再任京东东路都巡检。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　本年为青州老儒生刘盖筑室供居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　本年在州南瀑布涧侧建亭，人称富相亭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　青州民为之建富公祠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年9月27日</a>　以明堂典拜礼部侍郎。<br /></div>
-----end

汝阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0208103f3cb04cba9e9a7e6770bcd871_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0208103f3cb04cba9e9a7e6770bcd871");'><span id='0208103f3cb04cba9e9a7e6770bcd871_link'
